Current Commentary

Key Points of Post-Disaster Reconstruction in Bandit Areas 28

Since our country began strictly suppressing bandits, bandit areas have been gradually recovered, and there is hope for complete elimination within a limited time. Therefore, the issue of post-disaster reconstruction cannot but be urgently considered. Here, based on our humble opinion, we list the major points as follows:

(1) Appeasing Refugees: Today, the military action to suppress the Red Army is not a battle for land, but a battle for the people. The first priority after the recovery of bandit areas is to appease refugees. The exact number of refugees should be thoroughly investigated. The method should be to first register in cities and towns in each province and places where refugees gather, noting the refugee's origin, age, family status, etc., in detail. If it is found that some people were forced to join the rebellion due to the Red bandits' coercion, they should be pardoned for their past actions and allowed to rehabilitate themselves. During the registration period, reception centers should also be established to send refugees back to their hometowns as soon as possible. Strong laborers can be employed in public works projects such as road construction and land reclamation. The elderly and weak should be properly assisted by the government.

(2) Strengthening Self-Defense: Bandit areas have just been recovered, and local supplies are difficult. It is difficult for large armies to be stationed there, so it is necessary to strengthen the people's self-defense capabilities. On the one hand, implement the Baojia system; on the other hand, strengthen defensive fortifications. The government has already promulgated regulations on the Baojia organization method, which extends from households to Jia, to Bao, to Lianbao, and to districts, reaching the county. The system is interconnected and responsive. However, there are not many counties in the bandit areas that can truly implement it. The abuse of power and oppression of villagers by Baojia chiefs is particularly appalling. The people only increase the burden on district offices, etc., without any practical benefit. Therefore, it is necessary to find ways to correct the selection of Baojia chiefs. Those with both courage and knowledge and who have received considerable training should be appointed. After selection, personnel should be secretly assessed at any time to prevent malpractices. The construction of walled villages has greatly contributed to the suppression of the Red Army this time. Any town with defensible terrain should build earthen forts as a place for nearby residents to store grain and provisions. Deep trenches should be dug around to prevent sneak attacks. Sentries should be posted outside the forts day and night, and night watches should be sounded inside the forts to prepare for emergencies. As for the passages that the Red bandits must pass through, tall buildings should be built. The foundation of the buildings should be on high ground and rocky ground to prevent the bandits from attacking from above or digging in from below. Soldiers should be stationed inside the buildings to defend. Bullets, gunpowder, food, firewood, and water should be stored as much as possible to prevent encirclement by ruthless bandits. The construction of the buildings is intended to restrict bandit activities. Even if there is an alarm, it can be quickly sealed off. It was previously heard that the construction of walled villages in the bandit areas of Jiangxi was quite poor. Only Leping County was considered excellent. Guixi was second. The rest were poorly constructed and not functional. Later, the chairman of the provincial government actively promoted it, and the results were considerable. After the disaster, the people in the bandit areas were unable to engage in this work, so it was necessary to rely on the government to plan and implement it.

(3) Reorganizing Land: The Red bandits were obsessed with Wang Mang's "equal land" system and implemented their land distribution policy, burning contracts, destroying land boundaries, thoroughly confiscating and thoroughly distributing land, destroying the foundation of the rural economy in bandit areas. The Nanchang Headquarters has formulated thirteen question-and-answer types of land treatment methods for the recovered bandit areas to explain. Its content is roughly as follows: (A) Maintaining the system of private land ownership, but implementing a limit on landlords, limiting the area of land they own from one hundred acres to a maximum of two hundred acres. Beyond the limit, in addition to paying ordinary land tax, they must also pay progressive income tax. (B) At the same time, using peaceful methods of land distribution based on population, so that all cultivators have land to cultivate. These two principles are in line with the times and await implementation. However, in areas that have been deeply affected by banditry, there must be a lot of land where boundaries have been completely destroyed and owners have died. How should it be distributed? It is not specified. We believe that in this situation, we can only take special measures to abolish the private land ownership system and distribute the land to farmers for cultivation. The detailed methods of public distribution can be determined by the Rural Reconstruction Committee.

(4) Educational Facilities: The Red bandits implemented Red education for the people in the bandit areas, forcing them to accept it to numb their thinking. The reason why the military actions to suppress the Red Army have repeatedly gained and lost may be due to the neglect of changing the thinking of the people in the bandit areas. To remedy this, we must start with educational facilities. First, we must strive to popularize education in terms of quantity. Second, we should widely recruit intellectuals from the bandit areas who have fled to various places and send them back to their hometowns. Intellectuals have always been respected in rural areas and are most powerful in changing customs.

Other aspects, such as promoting the rural economy, developing land and water transportation, clarifying officialdom, and improving people's hearts, are essential steps for the revitalization of China as a whole and are not limited to post-disaster reconstruction in bandit areas, so they will not be discussed here for the time being.

Russian Ambassador to the United States Expresses Willingness to Strive for Peace 29

Admits to Laying Double Tracks and Strengthening Transportation Capacity

Preserving Every Inch of Territory to Resist Foreign Aggression

The Soviet Russian Ambassador to the United States, Troyanovsky, gave a speech at the Foreign Affairs Association in Cincinnati, Ohio, stating that the Soviet Union is eager for peace, but will never lose an inch of territory for peace. The reason why I repeatedly discuss the issue of peace is that the danger of war is very great, and the international situation is as tense as in 1914. It can even be said that it is more tense than before the start of the European War. The militaristic spirit of some national authorities is even greater than at any time. If the next war unfortunately occurs, the tragic consequences will be beyond our prediction. However, the people of all countries do not have a war-like mentality. At present, the two mentalities of eagerness to try and hope for peace are competing. Before we have a solid guarantee, we cannot be fooled by vague promises of disarmament. Finally, the Soviet Russian ambassador also said that it is not entirely hopeless to strive for peace. The restoration of diplomatic relations between the United States and Russia is enough to consolidate peace and add a layer of protection to world peace. (Havas telegram on the 2nd)

Before giving a speech at the Foreign Affairs Association in Cincinnati, Ohio, the Soviet Russian ambassador to the United States made a statement to the press, stating, "We do not believe that democracy has died. What our country is practicing is a kind of complete democracy, in which economic equality and no class distinctions exist. Our country's production equipment cannot be regarded as private property. Stalin's power is indeed greater than that of others, but we do not regard him as a dictator. The reason why his power is greater is because his ability surpasses others. We must obey Stalin, no matter what his orders are. Although Stalin is supervised by the party, we still obey the command of one person. The Soviet Union has no possibility of compromise with capitalism. The basis of its economic system is that those who work more get more benefits, and it does not adopt the principle of absolute equality. The production equipment is also the property of the state." When talking about international issues, Troyanovsky said, "The situation in Europe is more tense than in 1914." He denied the rumor that the Soviet Union intends to go to war with Japan, but admitted the construction of double-track railways, saying that this is precisely to show that the Soviet Union has sufficient strength to deal with countries that threaten peace in the Far East. (According to reports in mid-March of this year, the Soviet Union, in order to prepare for the situation in the Far East, plans to lay a large railway across Siberia, parallel to the existing Siberian Railway.)

(Havas telegram on the 2nd)

America's Attitude Toward the Puppet State Causes Astonishment in London 40

The Declaration of Non-Recognition is Still Fresh in Our Minds

Nanjing Should Not Disrupt the International Front

(London) According to recent reports from Washington, the United States has shown a trend towards recognizing [Manchukuo], which has caused considerable surprise and doubt in European political circles. The US government denies this claim. However, the public firmly believes that the US attitude towards recognizing [Manchukuo] remains ambivalent. If the US decides to take steps to recognize [Manchukuo], the problems arising from this move will be numerous. First, the US action would put the League of Nations in a difficult position. On July 1, 1932, former US Secretary of State Henry Stimson stated in a note to China and Japan that the US would not recognize any system resulting from violations of the Kellogg-Briand Pact. Therefore, if the US were to recognize [Manchukuo], it would contradict this policy. To show solidarity with Stimson, the League of Nations issued a declaration on March 11, 1932. Although the content of the declaration was not entirely the same as the Kellogg-Briand Pact, it was generally similar. In the same year, the League of Nations also requested member states to refuse recognition of any treaty, agreement, or situation obtained by methods that violated the League of Nations Covenant. The League of Nations has exerted itself so much for the US, and now it is bound by this. Second, the US recognition of [Manchukuo] would be welcomed by Britain. Britain believes that the existence of [Manchukuo] will be long-lasting, and it will be difficult to shake Japan's dominance in Manchuria in the short term. Britain is very close to the League of Nations, so it does not want to violate the League of Nations' attitude towards [Manchukuo] and be the first to recognize it. However, Britain certainly hopes that the US will take steps to recognize [Manchukuo], as a precedent for them to follow in the future. It is reported that Germany is also considering the issue of recognizing [Manchukuo]. The tense relations between Germany and Russia have led to closer ties between Germany and Japan. According to recent reports, the German ambassador to Japan, Dirksca, will soon visit Shenyang and Harbin, seeking German trade opportunities in Manchuria, or even recognizing [Manchukuo]. Although Soviet Russia is suspicious of Japan and fears a joint Japanese-[Manchu] attack, in principle, Soviet Russia does not refuse to recognize [Manchukuo]. In fact, there are already Soviet consuls in [Manchukuo] conducting various negotiations with the [Manchukuo] authorities, as if the relationship between Soviet Russia and [Manchukuo] is already close. Conversely, [Manchukuo] has also sent consuls to various parts of Soviet Russia, and we have reason to believe that Soviet Russia has long been prepared to recognize [Manchukuo], using a non-aggression pact with Japan as an exchange condition. This type of pact is also what Japan and [Manchukuo] urgently want to sign with Kremlin. It is said that if Japan adheres to the promise of an open door policy in [Manchukuo], the news that the US may recognize [Manchukuo] is indeed credible. A London news agency traces the fact that the late President Roosevelt recognized Japan's annexation of Korea after 1910, and that today's President Roosevelt may take similar steps to recognize [Manchukuo]. Indirectly related to the issue of recognizing [Manchukuo] is the Philippine independence proposal made by Tydings and Mcduffie. The proposal stipulates that the US will gradually abandon the US Army and Navy bases on the island. Europe views this move by the US as a powerful action to improve US-Japan relations, and Britain also expresses its joy at this situation. Suspicion and hatred between Japan and the US make Britain's situation very difficult. Britain does not want to adopt a pro-Japanese policy to anger the US, nor does it want to stand on the same front as the US to provoke Japan's resentment, because Japan has become a strong commercial competitor to Britain today. If Japan makes a firm decision, it can also disrupt Britain's Far East markets. If US-Japan relations improve, Britain can avoid the difficulty of being caught in the middle. (National Telegram, 3rd)

Athens The Greek Upper House has today ratified the recently concluded Balkan Pact (the signatories of which are Greece, Turkey, Romania, and Yugoslavia). During the discussion of the Pact in the Upper House, the Greek Foreign Minister reported in detail on the entire process of negotiating the Pact, and said that he believed [Bulgaria] should eventually join. (National Telegram, 3rd)

Belgian New King Gains Popular Support 49

Brussels Leopold III, the new King of Belgium, has recently ascended the throne at the age of 32, after the death of the old King Albert in a mountaineering accident. All his administrative actions follow the old rules and regulations, which has won him great popular support. The new King is extremely egalitarian and sincere. When he was 14, the Great War broke out, and he participated in the war in the trenches. When Belgium was occupied by German troops, he argued with his father, the King, to fight again, unwilling to submit to humiliation. The Queen, formerly Princess Astrid of Sweden, often pushes her baby carriage along the streets of Belgium, as simple as a common woman. They married in 1926 and have been known as the most beloved princess of this generation. It was once rumored that she would be engaged to the Prince of Wales of England. The King and Queen married out of love, having met and danced together in Paris before their marriage. They now have one daughter and one son, the son being four years old and the current Crown Prince of Belgium. (National Telegram, 3rd)

Siamese King Praises Italian Premier's Achievements 50

Rome The King of Siam, after meeting with the Italian press, issued a statement saying that Rome has undergone a great transformation since the Fascist government came to power, and the beauty of the city is far from what it was in 1920 and 1924. Before leaving Italy, the King of Siam plans to visit various industries in Turin. He also said that ["Mussolini is a great political leader who can think about implementation for every issue, works tirelessly for the country, and can rule a great power with an iron fist."] The King of Siam is scheduled to go to Turin tonight. (Havas, 2nd)

Heinous Murder and Robbery Case Occurs in the United States 51

Six Corpses Found Horizontally in a Room

Bloody Clothing Yields Clues, Criminals Arrested

White Bluffs, Washington A heinous murder and robbery case was discovered here on Saturday. The victims were four men and two women. The police now have a clue: a plain-colored shirt stained with blood. Several known criminals have been detained for interrogation. On Saturday night, a man named Sanders heard a dog barking fiercely in his neighbor Fried's house. Peeking through the window, he saw three dogs locked in a Packard car in front of the door, and two corpses lying on the floor inside the house. Greatly alarmed, he notified the police station. The police entered the house and found four male and two female corpses. The walls were stained with blood. Some of the six people had been shot to death, some had been beaten to death with heavy objects, and two had their throats cut. The items in the house were scattered, and the furniture was mostly broken. There had been a fierce fight in the room. Upstairs, a white cat was the only eyewitness to the massacre. The police believe it was a robbery, as two diamond rings owned by Fried's mother, worth $1,500, were missing. According to police opinions today, the murderers intended to eliminate all witnesses, hence the massacre of many people. The bodies were moved to the morgue last night for examination. Afterwards, the police issued a radio broadcast to the public. This morning, a tailor brought a blood-stained shirt to the police station, saying that someone had brought it to him yesterday asking to have it cleaned, and described the person's appearance in detail. Based on his statement, the police have arrested several criminals for investigation. (Reuters, 2nd)

Icelandic Volcano Erupts 52

Eruptions Reach 3,000 Feet, Like a Fire Dragon

Ice Melts from Heat, River Waters Suddenly Become Torrents

Reykjavik, Iceland In recent days, the large Skatárjökull volcano in southeastern Iceland suddenly erupted, erupting extremely violently. However, according to reports received, due to the vast area and sparse population, there has been no loss of life. However, a large amount of ice from the Skatárjökull glacier was thrown into the Skatár River. The river was originally a small stream, with its water coming from boiling springs. However, due to the large chunks of ice being thrown in, it suddenly became a torrent, threatening to flood. Reykjavik is 200 miles from the volcano, but the eruption can be clearly seen, looking like a fire dragon, about 3,000 feet high. At night, the red light obscures the sky. Some have counted the number of eruptions, saying that there are as many as 78 in 20 minutes, and the underground tremors, like thunder, can also be heard here. (National Telegram, 2nd)

Hong Kong Sailing Ship Undertakes a Daring Long Voyage 53

Now Arrived at Bermuda

Bermuda The 30-ton sailing ship Taamarschan, which set sail from Hong Kong last May bound for England, is being navigated by five naval officers on holiday. Seized by curiosity, they undertook this daring long voyage. The ship arrived in Bermuda today from Nassau, Andros Island (in the northern Bahamas). After purchasing the necessary supplies, it will head directly to England in a few days. The ship was built in Hong Kong and was originally intended to participate in a race organized by the Royal Ocean Racing Club. (Reuters, 2nd)

The Resignation of Gu Renfa Approved by the Provincial Government 58

The Provincial Chairman to Temporarily Oversee Affairs

(Zhenjiang) Gu Renfa submitted his resignation to the provincial government, stating: "I, Renfa, with my mediocrity and lack of talent and knowledge, am grateful for your guidance. I have strived to serve, hoping not to fail in my duties. Unexpectedly, during an official trip, I received a telegram informing me of the affair in which Li Shuyun, from my humble home, had incited Liu Zhuomin, the dismissed head of the Second Branch Bureau of the Wuxi Public Security Bureau, to disobey orders and resist surrender, interfering with government and undermining discipline. I believed that the law should not favor relatives, as ancient teachings dictate. Therefore, I telegraphed to request that the woman be handed over to the court for investigation according to the law, and I requested punishment for myself. Some time has passed since then, and I have not received any clear instructions. Looking inward, I feel deeply ashamed. Rather than occupying a position without fulfilling its duties and failing to live up to your expectation, it is better for me to retreat and allow those with talent to serve, hoping to have the chance to repay your kindness in the future. Therefore, I implore you to forward this to the National Government, requesting permission to resign from my positions as a member of the Jiangsu Provincial Government and the head of the Civil Affairs Department. This will allow me to alleviate the blame for failing to properly manage my family and fulfill my desire to return to civilian life." On the third day, the provincial government decided to forward the resignation, and the chairman will temporarily oversee the department's affairs. (Third-day special dispatch)

A Travelogue of Xinjiang 87

By Our Special Correspondent, Geng Ya

Mourning Artifacts in the Ancient Capital

During my stay in Tianjin, I visited Mr. Zhang Boling, the president of Nankai University. He advised me [on the points to pay particular attention to when going to Xinjiang. From the perspective of the new province's environment, the first is the actual traffic situation, the second is the economic situation, and the third is the political situation and others. After all, convenient transportation and a vigorous economy are prerequisites for politics and everything else to improve. The so-called economy is the prerequisite for everything, and it is the core issue of all problems. There is no doubt that the world in the future will further evolve into a world of economics.] When asked about the school's funding situation and the number of students, he briefly replied, [The number of students is more than 400 in the university, 1,350 in the boys' high school, 300 in the girls' high school, and more than 200 in the girls' primary school. The annual expenditure is more than 600,000 yuan, with the university accounting for 400,000 yuan. The sources of funds are: one, the school's foundation; two, social donations; and three, government subsidies. In the past, all have been insufficient, and in the future, it will inevitably be difficult. The more developed the school, the greater the cost. The main reason is that the school upholds the educational goal, considers the students' level, and cannot admit too many examinees in the hope of increasing tuition income. The situation is almost the same as in the news industry. In order to fulfill the social education responsibilities, we must make some sacrifices.] Nanda is located eight li south of the city. The noise of the city is far away and cannot be heard. The scenery is quiet and very suitable for studying. The area is vast and can be developed in the future.

From Tianjin to Beiping, I took the Beining express train. The train came from Shanhaiguan and arrived at Tianjin Station at 3:45 PM. It departed for Beiping at 4:00 PM and arrived at 7:00 PM. There were several Japanese officers on board. Many Japanese people, soldiers stationed in Tianjin, and representatives of Chinese organizations welcomed and saw them off. There were four ticket inspectors, half of whom were Westerners. However, they did not use scissors and were not heard to speak Chinese. They walked ahead proudly. Many people called them [foreign ticket inspectors]. Mr. Wang, who was sitting nearby, asked a Chinese ticket clipper, [What is the monthly salary of those foreigners?] He replied, [350 yuan]. He asked again, [How much do you make, sir?] He replied, [Chinese ticket inspectors make from 35 to 70 yuan. Some make 90 yuan, but those are senior supervisors.] A person holding a free pass said, [The highest salary for foreign employees of the Beining Railway is that of someone in the Transportation Department, who makes 2,000 yuan a month. Hiring senior foreign employees is probably due to treaty relations. As for the additional employment of foreign ticket inspectors, it started after the Mukden Incident because many passengers claimed to be refugees or on official business and refused to buy tickets. Foreigners handle matters without regard to feelings, so they are hired to do this work.]

Mr. Wang continued, [Not long ago, the survey team for the Xin-Sui Highway, which was dispatched by the Railway Department, also appointed a Swede, an archaeologist named [Sven Hedin], as the team leader because Chinese were not competent enough. He planned to enter Xinjiang for archaeology for the third time, so he was specially appointed as the team leader, and the Beining Railway Bureau advanced 40,000 yuan for his salary. I heard that there are recent achievements in Beijing, [a new route has been discovered, which is 50 li shorter than the old route used by the Xin-Sui Long-Distance Bus Company.] However, foreign newspapers reported the news of this trip, without understanding the truth, and many headlines were [Sven Hedin's Expedition to Suiyuan and Xinjiang], which is very different from the original meaning. Those who heard it were surprised.

Looking out the window, suddenly there was a vast expanse of water, with thin ice near the edge. The train passed over it, and it trembled. Suddenly there were several flat houses, with dust piled on the roofs. The wild wind swirled up and down. Although the fields have been cultivated, there is no green at all. The climate north of the Yellow River is much colder than in the south. The crops are wheat, sorghum, millet, and corn. If the rainfall is even, they can be planted three times in two years. The wheat sown after the white dew in the last autumn had already sprouted two or three inches, but it withered due to the winter cold and must wait for the spring to warm up before it can grow again and mature in the summer, which is faster than spring planting. After passing through Langfang, the earth is round and no mountains can be seen. This kind of plain landscape is evident once you cross the Yellow River border. As the sun sets, a thin layer of white like frost spreads all over the ground. Its material is either salt or alkali. I arrived in the ancient capital in the evening and stayed at the Beichen Palace.

I have visited the Liulichang and the East and West Single Markets. The market seems to be more lively than in previous years. Japanese goods are everywhere. A certain gentleman read in the newspaper [the Beijing Anti-Japanese Association investigated and burned Japanese goods in the Confucius Temple] and was horrified. When asked why, he replied, [The front line of national defense is the special environment of Beiping and Tianjin, just like the recent strong winds, which blow the soil and dust. The wind helps the soil, and the soil helps the wind. It is really hard to describe the depression of the yellow sky and gray earth.

The city of Beiping is full of gray dust, and the wind is even worse. In order to prevent pedestrians from falling into the five-mile fog, street cleaners constantly sprinkle water, but the wind blows and the sun shines, and it is immediately ineffective. Moreover, the remote streets and alleys are mostly piled with coal ash. In the area of Nei Dong Shuncheng Street, the pile of soil is as high as the city wall, so there was a statistic in the past that [it cannot be completely transported away in twelve years]. Now, the city government is planning to tidy up the city's appearance and has discussed with various bureaus to build a light rail to facilitate the removal. There is still a lot of accumulated soil in other places, and we should continue to clean it up. The fundamental solution is to urgently repair solid roads and ban the piling of dirty soil everywhere, so that the East Legation, which is the only one who is so proud, will not be able to remain proud forever.

A Corner of the Temple of Heaven in Beiping 88

Walking to the Xiannongtan and the Temple of Heaven outside Qianmen, the palaces and terraces are magnificent, and the ancient cypresses soaring into the sky are particularly rare. Because the cypresses were planted in the Yuan and Ming dynasties, they are all living trees that two or three people can encircle. Ancient relics, scenery, and city appearance are all important. Recently, there has been a lot of logging. Going forward to investigate carefully, you can see that only one root has two plants, and one of them has been sawed off. If you go to a certain side or a whole piece, dig it up by the roots, it is difficult to find. I heard that a total of more than 330 cypresses have been stolen from each altar, worth more than 150,000 yuan. There is a [Guan Geng Terrace] in the Xiannongtan. It was a wooden frame in the Ming Dynasty, but Emperor Qianlong of the Qing Dynasty changed it to a brick and stone structure for the emperor to watch his officials plowing to the end of the field after personally plowing. In front of the platform is the [site of the imperial plowing]. It is said that the emperors of the Ming and Qing dynasties performed the ritual of offering sacrifices to the Xiannong every year, and then personally plowed here. The ritual was performed by an old farmer of Shuntian Prefecture, wearing a coir raincoat and hat and leading an ox. The emperor wore a yellow dragon robe, held the plow on the right, and held the whip on the left. In the Ming Dynasty, he pushed three times and returned three times. After Emperor Yongzheng of the Qing Dynasty, he pushed four times and returned four times. The governor of Shuntian Prefecture carried a green box, and the vice-minister of the Ministry of Revenue sowed seeds. After the ceremony, the emperor watched from the [Guan Geng Terrace], and the farmer still had to finish plowing the field, which was both illusory and interesting. The scale of the Temple of Heaven is larger than that of the Xiannongtan. There is a [No. 21 Middle School] inside, and there are also troops stationed there, living in the halls. I only visited the Qinian Gate, the Qinian Hall, and the Huangqiongyu. The Qinian Hall is built on a circular high platform, which is divided into three levels, with a total of twenty-seven steps. The steps on the front are inlaid with three large carved stones. The lower level is clouds, the middle level is phoenix, and the upper level is dragon, all of which are extremely exquisite. There is a wooden sign in front of the tree, which says [Protect the carved stones, please walk on both sides]. At that time, there were four Japanese men and women, and one of them stepped on the carved stones and climbed up. I remembered that when I visited the [Beiling] in Shenyang in the 19th year of the Republic, I also saw Japanese people doing this. Looking back on the past, I couldn't help but feel sad.

Northeastern Railways Under Japanese Control (Changchun Correspondence) 92

The Northeast relies almost entirely on railways for transportation due to its scarcity of rivers and coastlines. The construction of the Northeast railways dates back several decades, and the development of the Northeast has also taken place over several decades. Therefore, it would not be an exaggeration to say that the history of Northeast railway construction is the history of Northeast development.

Since the September 18th Incident, the railway situation in the Northeast has been very different than before. Not only did Japan build many new trunk lines to cope with the current tense situation in the Far East, such as the Dundu, Labin, and Kehai lines, establishing three major trunk line systems (namely, one from Dalian via the South Manchuria Railway, two from the Korean West Line via Pyongyang and Seoul, and three from the Jingtun Line via the Sea of Japan), but also its management rights have undergone tremendous changes.

Before the outbreak of the September 18th Incident, the Northeast railway management system could be summarized into the following three types:

1. State-owned railways under the leadership of the Northeast Communications Committee of our country.

2. The South Manchuria Railway and its branch lines under the leadership of the Japanese South Manchuria Railway Company.

3. The Sino-Soviet joint venture, the Chinese Eastern Railway, and its branch lines.

Now, except for the second item, the Japanese South Manchuria Railway, which has not undergone major changes, the Sino-Soviet joint venture, the Chinese Eastern Railway, under the threat of Japanese iron hooves (such as the unwarranted detention of Soviet employees, etc.), the Soviet Union was forced to consider transferring the railway to Japan. Not long ago, Japan even held a so-called railway purchase conference to carry out this matter. As for our state-owned railways, they were entrusted to the management of the South Manchuria Railway by the puppet Ministry of Communications on March 1st of last year. The South Manchuria Railway established the so-called [Railway Bureau] to specialize in this matter. Its excuse was once declared to be to unify the management of the Northeast railways in order to engage in rational management, so that economic and technical efficiency could be improved. In fact, this kind of cover-up is precisely a case of trying to hide what is already obvious. Before September 18th, our state-owned railways, under the leadership of the Communications Committee, were extensively constructed. In a few years, using domestic capital and technology, the Hu-Hai, Qi-Ke, Shen-Hai, and Ji-Hai railways, totaling 893 kilometers in length, were built, adopting a strategy of surrounding the South Manchuria Railway. Huludao was built to compete with Dalian, and a joint transportation system was established, reducing transportation costs, causing the number of goods transported by the South Manchuria Railway to plummet. In addition, our Northeast authorities placed obstacles everywhere, so the South Manchuria Railway was almost in a dead end in this environment. The outbreak of the Northeast Incident was largely due to this. Therefore, this time Japan forced the puppet organization to hand over the management rights of the railways to avoid repeating the same mistakes in the future. Moreover, transportation is the lifeblood of a country. With the lifeblood in the hands of the Japanese, there is no need to worry about further changes. And when facing war against the Soviet Union and us, it can use the three major trunk line systems to quickly transport troops to seize the initiative. This plan is extremely sinister.

As for our state-owned railways under the management of the so-called [Railway Bureau], there are about ten lines in total, and their names are as follows:

1. The Guandong section of the Fengshan Line, Beining Railway, was renamed Fengshan after being occupied by the Japanese, starting from Shanhaiguan and ending in Shenyang. Its branch lines include Jinzhou to Beipiao, Dahushan to Tongliao, etc.

2. The Shenhai Line, starting from Shenyang and ending in Hailong, is a line built entirely with domestic capital and technology. After the Northeast Incident, it was once managed by a railway security maintenance association organized by traitors.

3. The Jihai Line. When this line was being built, the Japanese protested, claiming that it ran parallel to the South Manchuria Railway. Our country ignored this protest, which lacked reasonable grounds, and eventually completed it.

4. The Jichang Line, starting from Changchun and ending in Yongji.

5. The Jidun Line, from Yongji to Dunhua, is a part of the famous [Jihui Railway].

6. The Duntu Line, from Dunhua to Tumen, is also a part of Jihui. Before September 18th, it could not be built due to our country's obstruction. After Japan forcibly occupied the Northeast, it accelerated its completion and is now open to traffic. The above three lines (Jichang, Jidun, and Duntu) form a straight line, so there is also a name called the Jingtun Line, which is from the puppet capital Changchun to Tumen.

7. The Sitao Line. This line is composed of three lines: Sipingjie to Zhengjiatun, Zhengjiatun to Tongliao, and Zhengjiatun to Taonan. Its shape resembles a fork.

8. The Taoang Line, from Angangxi to Taonan, is 224 kilometers long.

9. The Taosuo Line, from Taoan to Solun, has only completed the Taoan to Huaiyuanzhen section due to financial difficulties.

10. The Qike Line, from Angangxi to Keshanzhen, with the Qiqihar to Keshan section completed not long ago.

11. The Huhai Line, from Hailun to Majiachuan Kou (close to Harbin) south of Hulan, is over 221 kilometers long.

12. The Labin Line, starting from Lafa and ending in Harbin (Binjiang), is 268 li long.

13. The Kehai Line, from Keshan to Hailun, is 167 kilometers long. This line and the Labin and Duntu lines mentioned above were all recently built by the South Manchuria Railway under [contract].

The current situation of the Northeast railways is roughly as described above. As for other matters such as railway security, it is controlled by the Japanese Kwantung Army based on the so-called [Japan-Manchukuo Agreement] and also by the Railway Bureau organized by the Japanese. As for its policy, because the railway is a frequent target of attacks by our righteous army, and the area is vast and difficult to guard, the following countermeasures have been decided: (1) Change the departure times of passenger trains at any time, and implement a [pioneer car] system when departing to verify whether the track has been damaged. (2) Implement war equipment in the car. (3) Strictly prevent our righteous army from mixing into the car. (4) Deploy an intelligence network to report the whereabouts and actions of the righteous army. (5) Complete communication equipment to facilitate rescue. (6) Investigate the actual situation of dangerous areas. (7) Increase railway security capabilities. (8) Build [railway protection villages] and provide small favors to villages near the railway to make them guard the railway. However, because the route is too long, and the righteous army is agile, appearing and disappearing unpredictably, it has not achieved complete results. (March 23rd)

The Executive Yuan Promulgates the Land Administration Outline 94

Ordering all provinces and cities to follow it for establishing bureaus, surveying,

Registering, assessing, and planning to collect land value tax

The Ministry of Interior recently felt that the land administration of all counties and cities needed to be carried out urgently. Therefore, it drafted a general outline of the procedures for provinces and cities to carry out land administration, as a standard for provinces and cities to carry out land administration before the Land Law is implemented, and submitted it to the Executive Yuan, which convened the Ministry of Finance, the Ministry of Judicial Administration, and many experts to review and pass it. It is heard that the Executive Yuan has issued an order to all provinces and cities to implement it. The outline is recorded as follows:

Land Administration Agencies

(A) Land Administration Agencies, (2) Administrative Agencies, 1. Land administration matters in all provinces and cities shall be temporarily designed and handled concurrently by the Department of Civil Affairs or the Bureau of Finance. When necessary, a Land Bureau may be established, directly under the provincial and municipal governments. 2. The provincial and municipal land bureaus shall each have a director, who shall be selected from specialized personnel. The director of the provincial land bureau may be concurrently held by the director of the Department of Civil Affairs when necessary. 3. The Land Bureau may be divided into two or three sections, each with a section chief, three to five staff members, and one secretary, one to three technical experts, two to six technicians, and up to sixteen employees. When necessary, land surveying teams and registration offices may be established. 4. The salary of the section chief, secretary, and technical expert in the preceding article shall be based on recommendation, and the salary of the staff and technician shall be based on appointment. (2) Land Adjudication Agencies, 1. Before the establishment of land adjudication courts at all levels, disputes over land rights shall be temporarily accepted by courts at all levels or county governments concurrently handling judicial affairs. 2. Property disputes arising during the measurement and registration process may be mediated by the competent land administration agency. (3) Evaluation Agencies, 1. The estimation of land value shall be carried out by the Land Valuation Committee organized by the municipal and county governments. 2. The Land Valuation Committee shall be composed of one to three persons designated by the municipal and county governments, one to three experts hired, one representative of the local court, and two to five representatives of statutory groups. 3. The Land Valuation Committee shall have a chairman, who shall be concurrently held by the mayor or county magistrate.

Land Consolidation

(B) Land Consolidation, (1) Measurement, 1. Land measurement shall be carried out in accordance with the procedures of large and small measurement, control measurement, household measurement, and continuous map making. 2. In areas where large triangulation measurements have not been carried out, provinces and cities may submit a request to carry out small triangulation measurements in advance, and their side length must be at least 10 kilometers on average, and the side closure difference (i.e., the remaining error of the triangle) must not exceed 12 seconds. The difference between the calculated side and the technical survey side shall not exceed one five-thousandth. 3. Large triangulation measurements shall be planned and carried out by the Ministry of Interior together with the Land Survey Bureau of the General Staff Headquarters. (3) Small triangulation, control, and household measurement shall be carried out by each province and city formulating implementation rules and submitting them to the Ministry of Interior for approval before implementation. (2) Registration, 1. Land registration must be carried out by submitting it to the competent land administration agency when the cadastral measurement of a certain area is completed. 2. Land registration must be carried out in accordance with the procedures in Chapter 3 of Part 2 of the Land Law. 3. The amount of registration fee and title certificate fee shall not exceed the provisions of each article in Chapter 4 of Chapter 3 of the Land Law.

Handling Price and Tax

(C) Land Tax, (1) The date of commencement of land tax collection. After the formal measurement and registration of each county and city is completed, a request may be submitted for the implementation of land value tax. (2) Evaluation Procedure, 1. The estimation of land value shall be based on the principle of zoning and classification. 2. For land considered to be in the same land value zone, the standard land value shall be estimated with reference to the land value declared by the people and the recent market price. 3. Land may be increased or decreased appropriately according to its standard land value depending on its special circumstances. 4. The estimation of land value shall be in mu as a unit. 5. After the standard land value is estimated, it shall be announced by the municipal and county governments. The same applies to land with special circumstances after it is estimated. 6. Within 30 days from the date of announcement of the standard land value, if the land owner has any objection, he may jointly sign with more than half of the people in the same land value zone and state the reasons in detail to apply for re-evaluation. For land value in special circumstances, if the land owner has any objection during the announcement period, he may apply for re-evaluation alone. 7. If there is still an objection after the standard land value has been re-evaluated, a request may be made for public judgment in accordance with the procedures of Articles 248 to 254 of the Land Law. (3) Tax Rate. The land value tax rate shall not exceed the provisions of Articles 291 to 296 of the Land Law.

Director of Jiangsu Finance Department Discusses the Situation of Jiangsu Province's Financial Reorganization 95

The Reorganization Over the Past Half Year is Gradually Getting on the Right Track

Improving the Accounting System and Eliminating Embezzlement

Zhenjiang Correspondence: Jiangsu's finances have always been notoriously difficult. Since the reorganization of the provincial government last year, reorganizing finances has been regarded as one of the most important tasks. Since its implementation, the results have been remarkable. The improvement of accounting and the determination of the budget have been valued by all sectors of society. Recently, according to Zhao Dihua, Director of the Finance Department, regarding the situation over the past six months, it is urgently recorded on the left.

Jiangsu Province has always been known as the wealthy area in the southeast. In recent years, both the provincial and county levels have felt that income is insufficient to cover expenses. Year after year, the accumulated deficit is very large. In the observation of a group of financial managers, they either say that income is short or that expenditure is huge, and that increasing income and reducing expenditure is the most important plan for reorganizing finances. However, at the present time when the rural economy is declining, the burden on the people is already heavy. If we increase the unified tax or launch a new tax, it will be difficult to do so. As for the expenditure side, it has already been extremely tightened. There are still many projects that have not been launched, and we must never give up eating for fear of choking. That is to say, there is no way to increase income and no way to reduce expenditure. If we want to solve the financial difficulties, we should eliminate embezzlement and stop waste. The reason why the province's finances are exhausted is not the shortage of income, but the embezzlement of clerks; not the complexity of expenditure, but the improper use of it. Therefore, using accounting methods to reorganize finances is really the most important thing for reorganizing Jiangsu Province today. Now, the financial reorganization situation in the six months since the establishment of this provincial government is described as follows:

Unifying Financial Administration

The province has a complex variety of special funds, and the competent authorities in each province cannot unify income and expenditure. The Finance Department loses its control over the special funds because it does not have jurisdiction over them. The competent department, on the other hand, is restricted by the administrative system for the collection agencies, making assessment difficult. Therefore, it is inevitable that they are separated from each other, and each county regards the special funds as extra income, arbitrarily misappropriating them. In this way, although there is the name of special funds, it is not enough to meet the needs of special projects. The provincial government meeting has previously proposed and resolved a unified method. Except for special education funds, which have separate regulations, all other special funds shall be handed over to the treasury. The Finance Department shall then jointly issue payment orders with the competent department in accordance with the budget, and the treasury shall pay them. It has been implemented for four months now, and the income from various special funds has improved significantly compared to before.

Establishing an Accounting Director

Counties have not followed the rules for bookkeeping and reporting for various income and expenditure items. The reason for this may be that the county government affairs are too busy and its energy cannot be focused, or that the county government's funds are limited and talent cannot be concentrated. Since December of last year, accounting directors have been established in counties with higher tax revenue, totaling 22 counties, specializing in bookkeeping and auditing county government income and expenditure items. Although they are not responsible for cash receipt, payment, and custody, they are responsible for urging the clearance of provincial funds and the deposit of county funds. Since their assignment, the accumulated funds in each county have gradually decreased, the treasury system has been established, and the accounting organization has gradually become perfect.

Establishing a Provincial Budget

The province's budget for the 22nd year was not determined before the start of the year, and there was no standard for the annual income and expenditure. After the establishment of this provincial government, three months after the start of the year, we adopted the principle of full collection and full payment, and the principle of adapting expenditure to income. We repeatedly discussed with various departments and bureaus and received their approval to reduce uneconomical expenditures and deferrable projects, and determined the estimate. The difference between income and expenditure was not large. Up to the present, except that the expenditure side has been implemented in accordance with the budget, the income items are very close to the budget number. The malpractice of false income and actual expenditure can be reduced (as of the end of February of this year, 66% of the land tax, 65% of the business tax, and 64% of the deed tax were collected).

Reviewing County Budgets

The local budgets of each county in the province are fragmented, complicated, and insufficient. For every matter, an additional tax is added, so that the additional taxes in each county often exceed the regular tax. Although there are a small number of counties where the excessiveness of additional taxes is particularly obvious because the regular tax is too low, the complexity of additional taxes cannot be denied. Moreover, the increase in additional taxes is often collected rashly by the county without waiting for the approval of the Finance Department, which is even more inappropriate. The provincial government committee has previously proposed and resolved to organize a County Local Budget Review Committee. First, the county magistrate of each county shall convene a local meeting to study the methods of review and reduction, and then the county magistrate of each county shall bring the draft budget for the 22nd year to the province separately, and each department shall send personnel to attend and jointly review it, so that each department can understand the local financial situation of each county, and the review standards can be used to delete and change uneconomical expenditures and expendable expenses, in order to prevent the false spending of funds. We started reviewing the budget last December, and we can complete it in early April. At the same time, the review of the 22nd year budget of each county will be used as the standard for approving the 23rd year budget.

Implementing the Audit System

After the provincial and county budgets are determined, the key to its effective implementation lies in whether the audit system is sound or not. Please state the following three points: (1) Regarding the implementation of the budget, the provincial audit system has always been lacking. Although the funds of each agency are issued according to the budget, whether the actual expenditure situation meets the budget and whether there is any waste has never been supervised by a legal agency. Therefore, in order to promote its implementation after the provincial budget is determined, it is necessary to establish an audit agency. This matter has been approved by the provincial government committee to establish an Audit Committee. The members of the committee will be selected from specialized talents by the provincial government to serve as a purely detached agency responsible for auditing the income and expenditure of provincial funds. (2) Regarding the implementation of the county budget, after the county local budget is reviewed and determined by the department, only part of the pre-supervision work is completed. As for whether each county is implementing it in accordance with the approved budget, it is necessary to supervise all income and expenditure statements and annual final accounts of each county, that is, the Finance Department will audit the county funds and use them in the county. The Finance Department will also be in a detached position to perform supervision. (3) Regarding the establishment of the county treasury, the funds collected by each county are mostly deposited in local money shops and businesses, which is inconvenient for auditing and prone to malpractices. Therefore, the provincial government committee resolved the method of collecting, paying, and depositing county funds in each county. All county taxes collected by each county government shall be handed over to the fund property office for deposit in the treasury designated by the Finance Department. Each agency shall issue payment orders after the county magistrate verifies and fills them out, and then the accounting director and the director of the public fund and property management office shall audit and stamp them before paying them to the treasury. In this way, the income and expenditure of county funds will be on track.

After implementing the above-mentioned points one by one, the income and expenditure will be centralized, the accounting will be independent, and the funds collected by each agency and each county government will not be misappropriated. Not only the provincial treasury can be enriched, but also the local funds will not feel exhausted at times. The finances of the entire province will be on the right track. At the same time, each county is also handling land reporting. On the one hand, we are reorganizing the provincial and local finances through the accounting system, and on the other hand, we are eliminating long-standing malpractices and reducing the burden on the people by handling land reporting. If we promote it for a year, our Jiangsu finances may gradually be reorganized. (National News Agency)

Zhongshan Hall Opens Today

The people of Suzhou have raised over 30,000 yuan and built a Zhongshan Memorial Hall with a large scale on the old site of the Mi Luo Bao Pavilion in Xuanmiao Temple. It is now scheduled to hold an opening ceremony this morning (4th) and hold entertainment in the afternoon. The Construction Department has specially telegraphed County Magistrate Zou to attend and represent the Construction Department.

Songjiang

Song People Initiate New Guang Electric Company

Although various sectors of society have successively submitted requests to the Construction Committee and the Electric Power Industry Guidance Committee to urge improvement, they have not been able to awaken them, and they have fallen into a state where improvement is impossible. I have recently learned that local people such as Lu Guixiang have organized a New Guang Electric Co., Ltd. The news I have obtained is recorded as follows: The company is organized as a service limited company with a total capital of 300,000 yuan, divided into 6,000 shares, each share worth 50 yuan. In addition to the fact that half of the shares have been subscribed by the founders, the remaining 150,000 yuan will also be the responsibility of the founders to raise the full amount after the Construction Committee approves it. All the company's articles of association, feasibility study, budget, and engineering design drawings were also submitted to the National Government Construction Committee, Jiangsu Construction Department, and Songjiang County Government for filing yesterday. A preparatory office will be set up in the County Education Association first. Mr. Lu is a graduate of the Department of Electrical Engineering of Beijing Jiaotong University and was sent by the Ministry of Communications to practice in the French Varouban雷 Wireless Electric Factory. After returning to China, he served as Section Chief of the Ministry of Communications, Director of the Radio Management Office of the Ministry of Communications, Factory Director of the Telecommunications Machinery Manufacturing Factory, and Director of the International Telecommunications Bureau. He is a domestic electrical expert. I met with the founder, Mr. Shen Lianbi, yesterday. According to him, since the conflict between the new and old managers of the Songjiang Electric Company occurred, although there have been many external criticisms, the internal disputes have not yet been resolved. For the sake of the future of public utilities, this organization must be established to assume the responsibility of the citizens. Knowing that this matter is significant, we should do our best to do it well. We hope that people from all walks of life will give guidance and supervision at any time so that it can be successful.

Continued Record of the Destruction of the Tinglin Public Security Bureau 96

Tinglin is the leading town in the county, and the business is prosperous. It is very close to Zhuanghang, Yanduntou, and Huan'an in the four villages. One evening, there was a race lamp meeting in Yanduntou, Shanyang, Zhuanghang, and other places, and Tinglin was the place where the lamps were gathered. First, a portrait of the president was used as a talisman by an eight-person shoulder sedan. Yang Meilin, the chief of the first branch, ordered the police in advance to block it at the Caishen Temple in the North City. The villagers bravely advanced. The police and the security team tried to stop them but they did not listen. They fired a volley into the air, but the villagers thought it was the president's portrait and were greatly angered. One sang and a hundred echoed, and the group rushed to the first branch and destroyed the bureau building. Yang Meilin, the chief of the branch, hid in the wheat field and was spared. The seals and guns were not lost. It is now known that the Public Security Bureau has reported to County Magistrate Jin and ordered Zhang Baoxiong, the chief of the twelfth district, to be responsible for repairing the bureau's houses and sending the ringleaders to justice.

Wuxi 97

Provincial Government Revises Regulations on Renting Factories

County Magistrate Yan Shenyu, due to the closure of several silk factories, including Huishengtai and Xin, in the county last year, which caused significant harm to society, found that the main reason for their closure was the lack of solid capital. They would rent a silk factory from the owner and start production. As soon as they encountered losses, they would close down. To avoid this danger, he passed temporary measures for prohibiting rented silk factories at the county administrative meeting on February 26th of this year, and reported it to the provincial government for record. The county government received instruction No. 616 from the provincial government the other day, saying: "Noted. The temporary measures for prohibiting rented silk factories that you have formulated are necessary and should be filed for record. However, the clause about depositing one month's wages as a guarantee does not comply with Article 25 of the Factory Law. Article 4 should be changed to: 'All operators who rent factories, after signing the lease, should deposit 20 yuan per silk reeling machine into the bank as a guarantee deposit, and submit the deposit slip to the silk factory association before being allowed to start operations,' etc., to comply with the legal system. This order must be followed." The revised temporary measures for prohibiting rented silk factories by the provincial government are appended below: Article 1: These measures apply to all silk factories operating in Wuxi County that rent factories. Article 2: Before signing a lease, all operators who rent factories should first submit the names of the operating shareholders and managers, the total capital, the name of the silk factory to be rented, the number of machines, and the location in writing to the silk factory association. The association will send personnel to verify the capital and report to the county government for record before they can sign a contract with the factory owner. Article 3: The total capital in the previous article shall be no less than 100 yuan per silk reeling machine. Article 4: All operators who rent factories, after signing the lease, should deposit 20 yuan per silk reeling machine into the bank as a guarantee deposit, and submit the deposit slip to the silk factory association before being allowed to start operations. Article 5: After receiving the guarantee deposit slip, the silk factory association shall issue a receipt and report to the county government for record. Article 6: When a rented silk factory declares closure, if there are no outstanding wages, the silk factory association should return the guarantee deposit slip based on the evidence after the closure takes effect, and report to the county government for record. Article 7: Those who violate the provisions of Articles 2 and 3 will be ordered to suspend operations after investigation. Article 8: These measures will be implemented after being approved by the provincial government.

Clash Between Police and Bandits in Baitangwei 98

Recently, water robberies have occurred frequently. The river surfaces of Gaoqiao, Baitangwei, and other places are vast, making them a haunt for bandits. A boat sailing from Wuxi to Jiaoxi (i.e., Jiaodian Town) in Wujin County the other day, owned by Huang Renda, carried more than a dozen passengers and cargo from Wuxi. When passing through Baitangwei, at around 9 p.m., it was suddenly approached by two bandit boats. More than a dozen bandits jumped out, each holding pistols, flashlights, and other weapons, shouting for the boat to stop. The boat had no choice but to stop and allow them to search and rob. As a result, they were robbed of 85 yuan in paper money, 2 yuan in silver dollars, 28 jiao in small silver coins, 4,000 copper coins, and two pieces of silk cloth, totaling more than 200 yuan in losses. After the robbery, the bandit boat encountered the first team of the county water patrol on the way and opened fire as a warning. The patrol boat also fired back immediately. For a while, the sound of gunfire crackled like a string of beads. After more than ten minutes of fierce fighting, the bandits were unable to resist and retreated. The patrol boat was unable to pursue due to the late hour and returned to the team to report to Captain Qian, who reported it to the county government for investigation.

Absolutely Will Not Yield to Any Force 99

Li Shuyun, wife of Gu Renfa, Director of the Civil Affairs Department of Jiangsu Province, and her mother, Li Liu, are suspected of instigating the case of Liu Zhuomin and his wife, the head of the Second Public Security Bureau, who disobeyed orders and resisted surrender. At the same time, Gu discovered that they were accepting bribes and engaging in fraudulent activities, which led to their arrest and imprisonment. The evidence of their crimes has also been collected by Gu and sent to the procuratorate of the county court for investigation. The procuratorate has scheduled a summons for Gu Renfa to appear in court on the 4th of this month (i.e., today) for questioning. This has been reported in this newspaper repeatedly. It is now known that Li Bingsheng, Li Shuyun's brother, came to Wuxi the night before last because he saw in the newspaper that she was ill in prison. Yesterday, he went to the detention center with Yu Tianxi, the director of the Wuxi office of lawyer Chao, to see Li Shuyun and her mother. When they met, they were overwhelmed by the contrast between the past and the present. Because they were tormented by illness, they were very thin. The mother and daughter wept incessantly while talking. Bingsheng comforted them a few words and left. He took a car back to his residence in Nanjing that night. In addition, Li Wen , Li Shuyun's cousin, was very worried when he heard that Shuyun was coughing up blood in prison. He took a car from Shanghai to Wuxi yesterday morning. After getting off the car, he went straight to the detention center to visit Li Shuyun and her mother. As Shuyun's condition had not improved, he planned to find a way to bail her out and take her to Shanghai for treatment. However, Li's condition had improved greatly in recent days, and she was in better spirits. She also stated that she did not want to be released from prison easily before the case was concluded. Therefore, Li Wenhua had no choice but to heed her wishes and no longer request bail for her. Yesterday, someone talked to Shuyun and asked if she could consider the old affection between husband and wife, not pursue the past, and reconcile, as there were rumors that Gu Renfa had hired a lawyer to conduct reconciliation negotiations with them. Li closed her eyes and frowned upon hearing this, and became very angry, saying, "What is this? Gu has been so cruel to me and has long forgotten the affection between husband and wife. Now, the outside world has a clear understanding of this matter. Although I am a weak woman, I still have some ambition and will absolutely not yield to any force. Gu's request for reconciliation is a dream. Even if he casts an image of me, Li Shuyun, and prostrates and kowtows three times and nine times every day, I would never bother to answer." Her pale cheeks suddenly turned red, showing the intensity of her anger.

Changzhou 100

Villagers Burn Down Wenchang Pavilion

The Houlie Temple in Lian Township, the seventh district of Wujin County, was scheduled to hold a welcoming god and temple fair on the 2nd. The county government, based on reports from various parties, requested a ban. It immediately sent Chief Police Officer Liu Shiqin and personnel from the Public Security Bureau to the countryside the day before to arrest the head of the fair, Yuan Yida. Other heads of the fair, knowing that things were not going well, went to the temple on the evening of the 1st and secretly stole the Sanmao Bodhisattvas and other statues out of the temple and hid them. When more than a thousand people arrived at the temple at 9 a.m. on the 2nd, preparing to welcome the gods, they suddenly saw that the bodhisattvas in the temple were missing. They first questioned the abbot monk, then tore down the portrait of the president of the primary school attached to the temple and placed it on the altar, planning to hold the temple fair. A teacher from the school came out to stop them and was beaten by the crowd. They also entered the school and drove out all the teachers and students. All the classrooms, desks, and chairs in the Wenchang Pavilion, as well as the teachers' clothes, bedding, and books upstairs, were piled up in the courtyard and set on fire. Soon, the fire spread to the houses, causing all six rooms upstairs and downstairs in the Wenchang Pavilion to be completely burned down. The crowd still wanted to cause trouble at the Hutangqiao District Office. After a flying report, the county government and the Public Security Bureau sent a team to the countryside to suppress them. Wang Liangsheng and other eight people were arrested and sent to the city that evening for interrogation by the county government.

Nanhui 101

Mistaken Arrest During Smoke Search Leads to Shooting Injury

In Sandun Town, the fourth district of the county, Wu Wenguang, an inspector from the Da Tuan Public Security Bureau, suddenly led more than ten police officers to search for opium dens the other night. They arrested one opium offender and were taking him back when a passerby, Pan Asi, coming from the south, caught sight of the armed police escorting a person. Suspecting it was a conscription, he immediately took off running. Wu and the others became suspicious and immediately chased after him. Asi, knowing it was difficult to escape, stopped. Wu and the others tied him up with a rope and forced him to go with them. Near Datuan Town, Xu Aguan, a mason, was returning home from work in the town when he encountered Wu and the others. Not understanding the situation, he inquired about the truth from bystanders. Feeling injustice that Asi was arrested for no reason, he expressed his dissatisfaction. Wu, hearing this, did not investigate and ordered the police to fire a warning shot, which hit Aguan in the shoulder, causing him to fall to the ground in pain, bleeding profusely. Seeing the trouble he had caused, Wu took the injured person to the town and sent him to Datuan Hospital for treatment. The county Public Security Bureau learned of the incident and immediately ordered Inspector He Yangwei to go to investigate the situation that night and take Wu and the police officers back to the bureau for verification.

Zhou was not against it, but Zhou's wife refused and forbade her husband from going there. Chairman's Speech

Chairman Wang Xiaolai gave a welcoming speech, saying: (Excerpt above) Mayor Shen has always taken the prosperity of Qingdao as his mission, and the colleagues of the various organizations present here today are also dedicated to the industrial and commercial sectors, seeking to develop the national economy and contribute to its improvement. Therefore, today's grand meeting can be regarded as a conversation meeting where like-minded people respond to each other, seek common ground, and express their aspirations. I dare to offer my humble opinion to Mayor Shen as a small suggestion. In recent years, the eastern province of northern China has been the most stable, and cotton, wheat, and peanuts are its main products. The raw materials needed by factories are generally available. Before the fall of the three northeastern provinces, many people from Shandong Province went to the northeast to make a living every year. Now that Shenyang has changed, this route has been cut off, and there is a danger of overpopulation. Qingdao has the convenience of water and land transportation, and there are abundant raw materials and surplus labor nearby. In the whole country, it is not only a commercial port for the distribution of goods, but also a rare industrial area. Today, Shanghai merchants are planning to make Qingdao a sales area, and it seems that they should go a step further and make Qingdao an investment area. This idea should be agreed upon by Mayor Shen and all of you present here. From another perspective, the Japanese military aggression has been successful, and they are taking a further step to seek so-called economic control. Last year, Japanese merchants held a meeting in northern China, and there was a proposal to make Qingdao the economic development center. At the same time, Japanese newspapers also proposed to cooperate with the Fuku Company to build a railway from Qingdao to the northwest. Therefore, although Qingdao is under the sovereignty of our country today, the Japanese, after being complacent in the northeast, are even more ambitious to covet it than before the return of Qingdao before 1922. If we do not seek our own interests, others will take our place. Preserving the rights and interests of Qingdao and seeking the prosperity of the city's economy is indirectly consolidating Qingdao's national defense. The key to this is something that must be explained to all of you present here. The crisis in northern China today lies in the fact that vagrants collude with traitors to incite the masses to cause trouble. If it succeeds, they will enjoy the benefits; if it fails, they will sacrifice the lives of our poor people as tools for their risky and opportunistic actions. There are too many unemployed poor people in our country, who are often willing to be used by these people for a price of ten or twenty yuan. This is evidenced by the recent case cracked in Qingdao. According to the confession of Sun Zuochen, the small leader, he used to work in the Zhongyuan Factory and later made a living by selling fish due to unemployment. He was tempted by the promise of thousands of yuan if the matter succeeded and went against his conscience. Therefore, to prevent the collusion of vagrants today, we must first stabilize people's livelihood so that they do not rebel to survive. Otherwise, the so-called traitors will be too numerous to be executed and too numerous to be arrested. The opinion of our association and others is that revitalizing Qingdao's industry is the way to ensure Qingdao's security. That is the idea. Fortunately, we met Mayor Shen in Shanghai, and the meeting was a good opportunity for cooperation between Qingdao and Shanghai. I would like to briefly describe my thoughts and await Mayor Shen's correction, and offer a toast to wish Mayor Shen success in benefiting Qingdao City, so that the prosperity of Qingdao City in the future will be on par with that of Shanghai, or even surpass it.

Shen's Reply 107

After the chairman finished speaking, Shen stood up and replied, saying: "I remember that I went to Ping thirteen years ago, and I went to Hangzhou fourteen years ago and passed through Shanghai. What I saw then is very different from today. The prosperity of Pudong today and the desolation of the past are the manifestations of the progress of Shanghai's commercial market. Furthermore, Shanghai is like the head of the body in the country, and everything depends on it. The competition among countries in the Shanghai market makes us unable to be optimistic. At the same time, if the rural areas in the country are bankrupt and we urgently seek to revitalize them, then the Shanghai financial community has the power to adjust the economy. We should enable Qingdao and Shanghai to communicate in the future, and the prosperity of Qingdao will depend on the support of Shanghai. I have gained a deep understanding of industry, commerce, and education through the provinces of Shandong, Henan, Anhui, Jiangsu, and Zhejiang during this trip south. Ultimately, they all take Shanghai as a model. In this understanding, I feel that (1) the organization of various parts of the country is unsound and the activities are not good, and (2) all industries, whether agricultural, industrial, or commercial, are outdated, resulting in slow progress in the future. When it comes to the Qingdao issue, we all have a painful history. After our country took over, there are now 15,000 foreigners, 4,000 to 5,000 Europeans and Americans, and a total of 20,000 foreigners in Qingdao. The relationship between Qingdao and the international community is constantly threatened by strong neighbors. It is my duty to do everything to protect the country and the people. As for the education and economic issues in Qingdao, let's not talk about education for now. What will happen to the Jiaoji Railway in the future, what about agriculture and commerce? Although I cannot be confident that the results will be good, I will uphold the government's prestige and take care of the people's interests, and I will do my best for the country. Nine years ago, the Economic Investigation Group went to Qingdao, and other groups went to Qingdao one after another, which fully demonstrated their concern for Qingdao. Although the situation in northern China is difficult at this time, and we are always in danger, I believe that if the whole country is willing to work hard and work together, it will not be difficult to overcome the difficulties. Finally, I would like to say that the transportation between Qingdao and Shanghai is very convenient now. I hope that you can come to Qingdao to guide us from time to time, and the future of Qingdao will surely progress day by day."

The Czech Consulate in Shanghai is Abolished 109

Consul General Rafa Will Return to His Country on the 12th

An Office Will Be Set Up Under the Jurisdiction of the Embassy

Shenshi News Agency reports that the Czechoslovak Consulate General in Shanghai, located at No. 50 Gubal Road, has recently received an order from its government to formally abolish it from April 1st. The Municipal Government has been notified. The affairs of the consulate have now been transferred to an office on Jiangxi Road, which is under the jurisdiction of the Czech Embassy. Dr. Rafa, the Consul General, has been ordered by the government to be transferred to Singapore as Consul General, and he is scheduled to return to his country on the 12th of this month. The Czech Consulate in Shanghai was established on April 1, 1931, and abolished on March 31, 1934, a period of three years. There are approximately 400 Czech expatriates, most of whom are engaged in the business of glass, crystal, electrical machinery, and armaments. It is said that the reason for the abolition of the consulate this time is to save expenses.
