A Large Batch of Tea Bricks from Our Country Are Shipped to Russia 112

Recently, More Than 7,000 Tons Have Been Shipped Out

The Value is Over Four Million Yuan

Dagong News Agency reports that tea bricks are a special product of our country. No other country competes in the Soviet Russian market, so the quantity exported to Russia is quite large. Since the end of last year, the Soviet Union has purchased no less than 10,000 tons of new and old tea bricks in our country, which is a very large amount. It is said that these large quantities of tea bricks are currently stored in warehouses in Shanghai, Hankou, and other places, waiting to be shipped to Russia by ship. Two Russian ships that entered the port the other day have already carried away more than 7,000 tons and set sail from Shanghai for Vladivostok, and then transshipped to Moscow. It is also said that the total value of these 7,000 tons of tea bricks is estimated to be over four million yuan.

Decline of Chinese Silk in England 113

Due to uneven silk quality and poor reeling techniques.

Japanese Silk Seizes the Chinese Silk Market in England

According to a recent announcement from the Guidance Department of the International Trade Bureau, the sales of Chinese raw silk in the United Kingdom have been declining year by year, while the sales of Japanese raw silk have been increasing annually. In 1930, Chinese silk sales were over 270,000 pounds, while Japanese silk sales were over 660,000 pounds. In 1931, Chinese silk sales increased to 320,000 pounds, but Japanese silk sales soared to over 1.21 million pounds. Last year, Chinese silk sales plummeted to just over 209,000 pounds, while Japanese silk sales surged to over 1.8 million pounds, accounting for more than half of the UK's total annual imports (the United States' total annual imports are over 2.36 million pounds). Within three years, the ratio between China and Japan has shifted from 1 to 3 to 1 to 10.

The reasons for the decline of Chinese silk are uneven silk quality. Eighty percent of raw silk imported into the UK is used to make women's silk stockings. Currently, most factories use Japanese silk. Furthermore, Chinese raw silk reeling techniques are poor, and British factories often have to re-spin Chinese raw silk, making it expensive and uneconomical. Recently, some Chinese silk producers have begun to imitate Japanese reeling methods, which are more popular. However, to improve raw silk, we must start with fundamentally improving silkworm breeds and rearing methods. The National Economic Council has recently hired experts to collaborate with provincial construction departments and agricultural colleges to reform silkworm breeds. After a few years, China's silk trade may be able to restore its former glory.

Over a hundred people attended, including Zhang Xianfang, Zhang Yichen, Chen Jicheng, Chen Jiufeng, Wei Zhiqiu, Jin Chutong, Hu Fengxiang, Cao Zhigong, and Wang Zhixiang. After the Jiangfeng Aircraft Accident 119

Wang Chonghong Flies to Wenzhou to Inspect

Xu Chengqi's Injuries Are Minor

The Jiangfeng Aircraft's Fuselage is Completely Destroyed

Dago News Agency reports that after the navy-made Jiangfeng aircraft crashed in Wenzhou and pilot Xu Chengqi was injured, the Shanghai Aircraft Manufacturing Plant received a telegram from Mr. Xu and immediately dispatched engineer Wang Chonghong to fly to Wenzhou to inspect the accident. The Navy also sent the Chutai warship to provide assistance. However, the aircraft fuselage was completely destroyed. Xu Chengqi's life is not in danger. The detailed information obtained is as follows:

Telegram Details 120

Engineer Wang Chonghong boarded the China National Aviation Corporation's Shanghai-Guangdong plane at 6:00 AM yesterday and arrived safely in Wenzhou at 8:10 AM. He immediately went to Datong Hospital to visit Mr. Xu. At 1:00 PM yesterday afternoon, Director Zeng Yijing of the plant received a telegram from engineer Wang stating: "To Director Zeng of the Gaochangmiao Aircraft Plant: Xu's condition is excellent. According to the doctor, there is no danger. Plan to return to Shanghai on the Chutai, but it has not yet arrived in Wenzhou. The aircraft is 50 li from Wenzhou. Have dispatched Guo Dian with workers and tools to dismantle it. Chonghong."

Fuselage Completely Destroyed 121

The Jiangfeng aircraft crashed in the Qilipu sandbar, 50 li from Wenzhou. The fuselage was completely destroyed. The nose and engine were embedded in the mud, and both wings were broken and scattered. After Director Zeng received the telegram from Mr. Wang, he immediately dispatched foreman Lin Guodian and two laborers to Wenzhou on the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Guangji to recover the wreckage.

Chutai Arrives in Wenzhou 122

After the Jiangfeng crashed from the sky in Wenzhou, the manufacturing plant immediately reported it to the Ministry of the Navy. The Navy then dispatched the Chutai warship stationed in Xiangshan to Wenzhou for rescue. After receiving the order, the warship immediately set sail and arrived in Wenzhou waters at 3:00 PM yesterday afternoon. Director Zeng told the Dago News Agency reporter that the Chutai will first arrange for Mr. Xu to be escorted to Shanghai for medical treatment. As for the Jiangfeng aircraft, it will be transported to Shanghai after the workers recover the parts.

Central Factory Inspection Bureau Decides on Factory Inspection Procedures 131

Progressing Sequentially in Five Phases

Municipal Government Orders the Social Affairs Bureau to Comply

The factory inspection issue has now been decided by the Central Factory Inspection Bureau. The implementation procedures for factory inspection will be promoted in five phases, submitted to the Ministry of Industry for approval, and an order sent to the Municipal Government for compliance. According to details obtained by a reporter from the New Sound News Agency, details are as follows:

Municipal Government Instruction 132

The Municipal Government instructed the Social Affairs Bureau, stating, "The Ministry of Industry's Central Factory Inspection Bureau's letter states, 'The decline of our country's industrial production has reached an extreme. Therefore, the Implementation Procedures for Factory Inspection have been formulated and submitted to the Ministry of Industry for approval. These procedures are formulated based on the general state of industry in our country as the basis for factory inspection, which seems extremely necessary. Please instruct your department to implement them conscientiously so that the entire Factory Law can be promoted as scheduled. However, before implementing these procedures, all work such as inspecting factory equipment and investigating worker conditions should be carried out first as preparation for implementation. Furthermore, the work of each phase specified in the procedures only outlines the key points. All implementation plans should be formulated in detail by local authorities with reference to the actual conditions of each locality. It is hoped that you will instruct your department to report the implementation plan for the first phase to the department within one month of receiving this document. Subsequently, the implementation plan for each phase should be submitted to the department for review three months before implementation. In addition to separate letters, a copy of the Implementation Procedures for Factory Inspection is enclosed, asking your government to instruct your department to conscientiously implement them. That is what is desired,' and attached a copy of the Implementation Procedures for Factory Inspection. Approved accordingly. A copy of the original document is hereby made and ordered to the bureau for compliance and reporting to be forwarded for verification. This order.'"

Implementation Procedures 133

Implementation Procedures for Factory Inspection: The Factory Law and the Factory Inspection Law have been promulgated successively and have been put into effect. This bureau, responsible for guiding and supervising national factory inspections, should naturally execute them in accordance with the law to see the results. However, at present, factory production in our country is not only backward but also declining. Therefore, after detailed review of the environment and needs of both labor and management, the Implementation Procedures for Factory Inspection have been formulated, adhering to the principle of gradual progress, classifying the clauses of the Factory Law according to their urgency and difficulty and determining the order of implementation. However, the clauses listed in the first phase of these procedures should continue to be inspected in the second phase. The rest can be inferred by analogy and must not be interrupted. The items that should be inspected in each phase must be completed before the implementation of the next phase to facilitate the advancement of the entire procedure.

Phase 1: (1) Matters concerning factory records: (A) Factories should establish factory records in accordance with the provisions of Articles 3 and 4 of the Factory Law and handle them in accordance with the law. (2) Matters concerning the work of child labor, female labor, and apprentices: (A) Factories should handle the work of child labor and female labor in accordance with the provisions of Articles 6 and 7 of the Factory Law. (B) Factories should handle the work of apprentices in accordance with the provisions of Article 59 of the Factory Law. (C) Factories should provide vocational training for apprentices in accordance with Article 65 of the Factory Law. (3) Matters concerning worker allowances and pensions: (A) Factories should handle injuries, illnesses, or deaths caused by performing duties in accordance with the provisions of Article 45 of the Factory Law (factory inspectors are only responsible for investigating injuries, illnesses, or deaths caused by workers performing duties when implementing this article). (4) Matters concerning disaster deaths and injuries: (A) If a disaster occurs in a factory or causes workers to die or be injured, it must be handled in accordance with the provisions of Article 48 of the Factory Law. (5) Matters concerning apprenticeship contracts and treatment: (A) When a factory hires apprentices, it should handle it in accordance with the provisions of Article 56 of the Factory Law. (B) During the apprenticeship period, accommodation, medical expenses, and allowances for apprentices should be handled in accordance with the provisions of Article 61 of the Factory Law. (6) Laws and regulations related to implementation and inspection: (A) All laws and regulations related to the items to be inspected should be strictly implemented. (7) Preparatory work for the last four phases of this procedure: (A) All items to be inspected in the last four phases of this procedure should be prepared.

Phase 2: (1) Matters concerning safety and health equipment: (A) Factories should handle safety and health equipment in accordance with the provisions of Articles 41 and 42 of the Factory Law. (B) Factories should provide training for workers to prevent disasters in accordance with the provisions of Article 43 of the Factory Law. (C) If the safety or health equipment of a factory is imperfect, the factory inspector should report it to the主管官署 in accordance with the provisions of Article 44 of the Factory Law. (2) Matters concerning the number of apprentices: (B) The number of apprentices recruited by factories should be handled in accordance with the provisions of Article 63 of the Factory Law. If the number recruited is too large, it should be handled in accordance with the provisions of Article 64 of the Factory Law. (3) Laws and regulations related to implementation and inspection: (A) All laws and regulations related to the items to be inspected should be strictly implemented. (4) Preparatory work for the last three phases of this procedure: (A) All items to be inspected in the last three phases of this procedure must be prepared. (5) Concerning the continued implementation of the items specified in the first phase of this procedure (A) All items that should be inspected as stipulated in the first phase of this procedure should continue to be inspected.

Phase 3: (1) Matters concerning working hours: (A) Factories that use a day and night shift system should handle it in accordance with the provisions of Article 9 of the Factory Law. (B) If working hours are extended due to natural disasters, accidents, or seasonal conditions, it should be handled in accordance with the provisions of Article 10 of the Factory Law. (C) The working hours of child labor should be handled in accordance with the provisions of Articles 11 and 12 of the Factory Law. (D) Apprentice working hours should be handled in accordance with the provisions of Article 58 of the Factory Law. (2) Matters concerning worker rest: (A) Rest during working hours should be handled by the factory in accordance with the provisions of Article 14 of the Factory Law. (B) One day of rest per week for trade unions should be handled in accordance with the provisions of Article 15 of the Factory Law. (C) Rest on commemorative days and holidays should be handled by the factory in accordance with the provisions of Article 16 of the Factory Law. (3) Matters concerning supplementary education for child labor, apprentices, and workers: (A) Supplementary education for child labor, apprentices, and workers should be handled in accordance with the provisions of Article 36 of the Factory Law. (4) Laws and regulations related to implementation and inspection: (A) All laws and regulations related to the items to be inspected should be strictly implemented. (5) Preparatory work for the last two phases of this procedure: (A) All items to be inspected in the last two phases should be prepared. (6) Concerning the continued implementation of the items specified in the previous two phases of this procedure: (A) All items that should be inspected as stipulated in the first and second phases of this procedure should continue to be inspected.

Phase 4: (1) Matters concerning the age of child labor: (A) Factories should handle the age of employed child labor in accordance with the provisions of Article 5 of the Factory Law. (B) The age of employed apprentices should be handled in accordance with the provisions of Article 57 of the Factory Law. (1) Matters concerning working hours: (A) Factories should handle the night work of female workers in accordance with the provisions of Article 13 of the Factory Law. (2) Matters concerning maternity leave for female workers: (A) Factories should handle maternity leave and pay for female workers in accordance with the provisions of Article 37 of the Factory Law. (4) Laws and regulations related to implementation and inspection: (A) All laws and regulations related to the items to be inspected should be strictly implemented. (5) Preparatory work for the fifth phase of this procedure: (A) All items to be inspected in the fifth phase of this procedure must be prepared. (6) Concerning the continued implementation of the items specified in the previous three phases of this procedure: (A) All items that should be inspected as stipulated in the first, second, and third phases of this procedure should continue to be inspected.

Phase 5: (1) Matters concerning working hours: (A) Factories should handle the working hours of adult workers in accordance with the provisions of Article 8 of the Factory Law. (2) Matters concerning worker leave: (A) Factories should handle special leave for workers in accordance with the provisions of Article 17 of the Factory Law. (3) Laws and regulations related to implementation and inspection: (A) All laws and regulations related to the items to be inspected should be strictly implemented. (4) Concerning the continued implementation of the items specified in the previous four phases of this procedure: (A) All items that should be inspected as stipulated in the first, second, third, and fourth phases of this procedure should continue to be inspected.

Shanghai West Sanitation Workers' Strike 134

Nineteen Workers Detained and Sent to the Bureau

Dago News Agency reports: Sanitation workers in the Shanghai West District earn only three to four yuan per month. Police劝阻 135

After receiving the order, the district sent police to advise the workers against it, but the workers, citing their difficult livelihoods, said that they could not obey.

Workers Arrested 136

The Reason for Adjusting Train Schedules on Two Lines 139

The new train schedules for the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo lines, which took effect on the first of this month, have been reported in this newspaper several times. It is said that the main reason for the railway authorities' revision of the schedules is the mandatory modification of the operating times of the Shanghai-Peiping through trains No. 301 and 302. Train No. 301 departs from Peiping at 3:05 PM and arrives in Shanghai at 7:55 AM on the third day. Train No. 302 departs from Shanghai at 4:05 PM and arrives in Peiping at 10:29 AM on the third day. The entire journey has been reduced from two days and two nights to two nights and one day, in order to save travel time between Shanghai and Peiping. At the same time, the schedules of all passenger trains on both lines have been re-arranged to meet current passenger transport needs. Its advantages, not found in previous schedule revisions, are three: (1) Major passenger trains on the Beijing-Shanghai line are connected with those on the Tianjin-Pukou line. In addition to the Shanghai-Peiping through train, such as the seventh Beijing-Shanghai express train and the first Tianjin-Pukou train, the fifth Beijing-Shanghai overnight express and the third Tianjin-Pukou train, the fourth Shanghai-Beijing express and the second Tianjin-Pukou train, and the sixth Shanghai-Beijing overnight express and the fourth Tianjin-Pukou express, are all connected. (2) Between Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou, in addition to the original Beijing-Zhapu through express train that continues to operate as usual, interval trains have been added. For example, the Beijing-Shanghai line's down train No. 15, the Zhenjiang-Shanghai mixed interval train, connects with the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo line's down train No. 41, the Shanghai-Jiaxing mixed interval train. The Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo line's up train No. 40, the Jiaxing-Shanghai mixed interval train, connects with the Beijing-Shanghai line's up train No. 16, the Shanghai-Zhenjiang mixed interval train. All use the same train cars to operate as a through train between Zhenjiang and Jiaxing, and passengers do not need to change tickets or trains at the North Shanghai Station. (3) The arrival times of major passenger trains on the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo lines are also connected. On the down direction, such as the Beijing-Shanghai line's train No. 5 connecting with the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo line's train No. 31, the Shanghai-Zhapu express train, and the seventh Beijing-Shanghai express connecting with the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo line's train No. 35, the Shanghai-Zhapu express. On the up direction, the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo line's train No. 36, the Zhapu-Shanghai express, and train No. 32, the Zhapu-Shanghai special express, are both connected with the Beijing-Shanghai line's sixth overnight express train. Furthermore, after train No. 301 arrives in Shanghai, it can connect with the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo line's train No. 33, the Shanghai-Zhapu express train. After the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo line's train No. 34, the Zhapu-Shanghai express train, arrives in Shanghai, it can connect with train No. 302, which is particularly convenient for passengers between Hangzhou and Shanghai. In addition, the up train No. 2, the Zhapu-Beijing through express, is advanced to depart from Zhapu at 7:45 AM, arrive in Shanghai at 12:25 PM, depart from Shanghai at 1:00 PM, and arrive in Beijing at 7:35 PM, which is two hours earlier than the previously scheduled time, to facilitate up-bound through passengers between Hangzhou, Shanghai, and Beijing. Also, the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo line's train No. 31, the Shanghai-Zhapu express train, which was originally scheduled to depart from Shanghai at 9:15 AM and arrive in Zhapu at 2:15 PM, is now changed to depart from Shanghai at 7:50 AM and arrive in Zhapu at 12:50 PM, an advance of one hour and twenty-five minutes, allowing passengers from Shanghai to Hangzhou and Zhapu to arrive earlier. Since the implementation of this timetable, travelers have praised its convenience.

Lu Xinggong's Coffin to be Transported to Shanghai Today 140

Burial at 3 PM

Lu Xinggong, a pioneer of the Chinese revolution, died of heart disease at his residence in Peiping on June 12 last year. At that time, because the Japanese bandits occupied North China and Peiping and Tianjin were in imminent danger, his family, in order to uphold the deceased's lifelong ambition of worrying about the country and forgetting personal matters, did not inform relatives and friends, so very few people outside knew about it. Now his family has scheduled to receive the post in Peiping on March 29, originally scheduled to transport the coffin to Shanghai on March 31, and bury it on April 3. It is now learned that a telegram from Peiping states that it is approved to arrive in Shanghai on April 4. On the same afternoon at 1 PM, the procession will depart from the North Station and be buried at 3 PM in the Shanghai Municipal Council Cemetery on Hongqiao Road.

The Chinese Jisheng Association, because on the evenings of March 5th and 6th, more than 1,700 thatched shacks were burned down in two locations in Zhabei, Pushan Road and Jingjiang Road. The association, together with the Zhabei Charity Group, jointly operated a congee distribution at the Liuying Road Congee Factory. Members were dispatched to investigate and issue congee vouchers. Terrible Fire Tragedy on Mongolian Branch Road 154

Zhu Zengjun Unaware of the Fire

Eight Men, Women, and Children Burned to Death

At 2:05 AM yesterday morning, a fire broke out in the overhanging building at the entrance of Lean Lane, Mongolian Branch Road, north of the Xinzha Bridge in Zhabei, and spread to a total of five buildings on the left and right, burning to death eight men, women, and children. The details are divided as follows:

Observation of the Fire Scene 155

Mongolian Branch Road is located north of the Xinzha Bridge, connecting Mongolian Road to the north and Kulun Road to the south. Lean Lane, in addition to the overhanging building, has more than 20 Japanese-style houses, all of which are low-rise buildings. Eight or nine out of ten residents are manual laborers. Each house is inhabited by two or three or four or five households. Moreover, this lane connects to Mongolian Branch Road to the east, but does not connect to the west, with only one entrance and exit usually. Therefore, it is very dangerous in the event of a fire.

Process of the Fire 156

At 2:05 AM yesterday morning, a fire alarm suddenly sounded in the overhanging building at the entrance of this lane. Neighbors on the left and right were awakened from their sleep. However, the residents of the lane were unable to escape, crying and shouting, and the order was in chaos. Fortunately, the police officer at the Wuzhen Road Police Station at that location learned of it early, reported to the Fire Department, and drove to the scene to extinguish the fire. It took more than an hour to extinguish the fire. When the fire was raging, most of the residents in the lane climbed onto the roofs to try to escape.

Men and Women Burned to Death 157

After the fire was extinguished, Yang Junfeng, an inspector from the Wuzhen Road Police Station, led police officers to investigate and learned that the front and rear floors of the overhanging building were inhabited by two families. The front floor was inhabited by Zhu Junzeng and others. Zhu's wife, Chen, Zhu's eldest son, Daqi, and second son, A'er, were all buried in the fire. The rear floor was inhabited by Chen Tingrong. Chen had a wife and four daughters, all of whom were burned to death. After the fire broke out, Zhu Junzeng learned of it early and jumped out of the window, and was arrested by the police. He is now in the Fourth District. Zhu had an elder brother named Junxiang, who was burned and was sent to the Chinese Red Cross Hospital by the fire truck for treatment. It is heard that he also died yesterday afternoon.

Ages and Origins of the Deceased 158

According to the reporter's investigation, Zhu Chen, the deceased, was 39 years old, Zhu's eldest son, Daqi, was 11 years old, and his second son, A'er, was 4 years old. Zhu Junxiang was 60 years old. Zhu, the husband of Chen, was from Yancheng. Chen Tingrong was 38 years old, from the northern countryside of Yangzhou. Chen's wife, Wang, was 40 years old. The eldest daughter, Da Long, was 7 years old, and the second daughter, Xiao Long, was 4 years old. Chen had three younger brothers, Tingfang, 35, Tinghe, 26, and Tingzhi, 24, all of whom worked as laborers at the Sanxin Trucking Company north of the Wuzhen Road Bridge with the deceased.

Autopsy Process 159

After the incident, Shen Xiaowu, the landlord of the Second Tu (formerly the Tenth Tu) in that area, was summoned by the Wuzhen Road Police Station of the Fourth District Public Security Bureau to report to the Shanghai District Court requesting an autopsy. At 5:20 PM, Prosecutor Cao Changlin, accompanied by Clerk Sun Shiquan, etc., verified that the deceased were all charred, with broken heads and rotten foreheads, or ruptured abdomens and flowing intestines, or completely charred, with blood and flesh dripping, which was unbearable to witness. He immediately ordered the preparation of coffins for collection and burial, and summoned Hu Yao, the police chief of the station, for questioning before leaving. Currently, the Chen family's bodies have been collected and buried by Chen Tingfang and the other two, while the Zhu family's bodies are still exposed at the entrance of the Mongolian Branch Road.

Police Report 160

The Wuzhen Road Police Station reported to the Fourth District, stating: Report regarding the matter. At 2:05 AM today (i.e., yesterday), a fire broke out for unknown reasons in the home of resident Zhu Junzeng at 62 Lean Lane, Mongolian Branch Road, in the overhanging building within the jurisdiction of this station. The number of deaths is as mentioned above, omitting the details.

Unaware of the Fire 161

Gasoline and Kerosene Prices Rise Across the Board Yesterday After the Imposition of Import Tariffs 162

Kerosene Up Eight Jiao Per Case

Dagong News reports that the four major kerosene companies in this city, Mobil, Texaco, Asia, and Oil Everywhere, believe that since China increased the import tax on gasoline from the first of this month, the cost of kerosene has increased. In order to avoid losses, they agreed yesterday to uniformly increase prices to make up for the loss of tax payments. The price of kerosene under the New Brand Happiness, Monk Cap, and Brand, etc., has increased by eight jiao per case (two cans). The original price of 6.4 yuan is now 7.2 yuan. Old brands such as Red Star and Yuanbao, etc., have also uniformly increased by eight jiao per case. Gasoline, which was originally sold for seven jiao per gallon, has now uniformly increased to eight jiao. It is planned to continue to increase prices in the future depending on market conditions. The price in the mainland will have to be increased due to water transportation and other miscellaneous expenses.

Recently, the defendant repeatedly called, wanting to borrow dozens of yuan, or else he would resort to considerable measures. He ignored him. On the 1st of this month, the defendant sent a letter in his name, asking to meet at the Shangbin Hotel. If he did not agree, he would announce his family's secrets in the newspapers. He then reported to the police station, and the detectives negotiated with the defendant and came to an agreement before arresting him. He replied that she was not. Then, he asked for the young master (i.e., Li Zuchao), and he still replied that he was not there. Questioned, the defendant confessed that he used to work in the Li family but was dismissed four or five years ago. Being unemployed and unable to make a living, he called Li from the Shangbin Hotel on the 26th of last month, asking to borrow dozens of yuan. Later, due to the lack of results, he wrote a letter stating that if Li did not agree to lend him money, he had no other choice but to commit suicide and write a suicide note for publication, so that everyone would know that he died because of this, and that it would also have a significant impact on Li's reputation. Finally, police lawyer Gan Jingxian rose to argue [omitted]. Judge Liu Yugui verified the confession and ordered the defendant to be detained, awaiting sentencing this week.

Reflections on Children's Day in the 23rd Year, by Pan Gongzhan 166

Those who speak of politics consider the people as one of the three essential elements of a nation. Ancient Chinese books also contain the saying, "The people are the foundation of the state." This is because the prosperity or decline of a nation depends on the strength of the national physique and the quality of its culture. The physique of adults is mostly fixed. Even if physical education is promoted to remedy their weakness, its usefulness is limited, and it is already too late. It is better to forge the physique of children. Furthermore, the knowledge of adults is nearly fixed, and the ignorant are often oppressed by poverty, toiling all day long without time for further study, and their brains are rigid and their memory is dull. It is not like children who are sensitive to impressions. Therefore, those who plan for the nation should first pay attention to children's affairs, to cultivate the foundation of the nation and place the country on a rock-solid foundation. Adults are the already-formed backbone of the nation, while children are the future lifeline of the nation. The importance of their position can be generally seen. Western powers all pay deep attention to children's affairs. The establishment of children's parks and children's libraries has become commonplace. Soviet Russia, as a socialist country, widely establishes nurseries to accommodate the children of farmers and workers, raising and nurturing them with utmost care. This is actively protecting children. Italy, as a fascist country, has the ambition to succeed Rome and dominate the world. Therefore, it specially rewards marriage and allows the firstborn children of all to be baptized in the cathedral. This is actively encouraging reproduction. Germany, after the Great War, suffered deeply, but its determination to seek revenge and revival has never ceased. Moreover, its domestic science is advanced, and all facilities tend to be scientific. In addition to actively training women's physiques, it has recently sterilized 400,000 men and women to select superior genes. These people are all mentally ill or have hereditary diseases. This is moving from active promotion to passive prevention, to cut off bad reproduction in future children. Such attention is given. Moreover, some countries still follow the ancient Spartan method of preserving and eliminating infants. Only China has never valued children's affairs and has never recognized the status of children. In humble self-reference, they do not say "piglet," but call them "puppy." If children are livestock, what status can be spoken of? Throughout China's thousands of years of history, I have never seen the government promote children's affairs, nor have I seen any measures to establish children's affairs. It is said that "after ten years of breeding and ten years of teaching," only King Goujian of Yue once had this affair of rewarding reproduction and paying attention to education. I have not seen another person who did this.

The current situation in China is not a concern about the lack of children but a concern about their lack of health. It is not a concern about the reward of reproduction but a concern about the lack of ways to protect them. Children are so weak, and the decline of the country follows. Therefore, to revitalize China, it is necessary for everyone to recognize the status of children, work hard to build children's affairs, and cultivate the foundation of the country. There are several aspects of affairs that should be carried out:

(1) Regarding the physical aspect of children, in the active aspect, such as paying attention to children's cleanliness and hygiene, promoting children's games and sports, and establishing or opening children's parks and sports fields, etc.; in the passive aspect, such as free medical treatment in hospitals and free physical examinations, etc.

(2) Regarding the intellectual aspect, such as founding children's newspapers and other publications, establishing children's libraries, holding children's lectures, showing children's educational films, and visiting zoos and museums, etc.

(3) Regarding the aspect of relief, such as promoting nursery services, establishing children's education and care homes, or delinquent children's reformatories, etc.

The affairs to be carried out cannot be fully listed. In short, children's affairs are related to the survival of the nation, the civilization or barbarism of society, and the rise or fall of the nation. They are extremely important and great. However, their effects cannot be seen in one or two years, nor can they be seen in five or ten years. It must be after twenty or thirty years. Moreover, their facilities are not sufficient for one village or one township, nor are they sufficient for one county or one province. They must be spread throughout the country. Because of the slowness of seeing results and the magnitude of their affairs, they are neglected by people. China has never regarded children's affairs as a national policy for thousands of years, and there is a reason for this. However, previous generations were all closed off, independent, and dignified. The culture of the four neighbors was very low, and they were all regarded as barbarians. Now, there is strife among nations, and the superior prevails over the inferior. If we do not work hard from the root, we will not be able to save the country from danger and ruin. On this happy Children's Day, in addition to commemorating and celebrating, how can we not pay attention to it?

Japan's Slavish Education in the Northeast 172

Rewriting Textbooks to Create Pro-Japanese Puppets

Raising Tuition to Resist Youth Enrollment

(Changchun Correspondence) Japan single-handedly controls the economy, politics, and military of the puppet state in the Northeast. Moreover, it is vigorously implementing its poisonous scheme of cultural aggression in the education of the puppet state. Because the strength of a country is fundamentally based on education, only by enslaving the education of the Northeast can Japan hope that the puppet state will be permanently under its control. Now, the details are collected as follows:

Rewriting Textbooks

Japan attaches great importance to secondary education in the puppet state. Regarding the teaching problem, it had previously elected a committee to specialize in collecting materials. Recently, a committee was held at a middle school in Fengtian. Based on the draft prepared by a member of the committee, other members were compiled and sorted out. It was completed in March of this year. Since the new semester in April, the textbook will be used. The various materials collected by the committee member actually exceeded 1,300 points, compared to the approximately 500 pages selected by the Dalian Committee. At the recent review meeting, 38 middle school principals served as members, and Kuribayashi, a school affairs official from the Japanese Kwantung Office, participated in the meeting. He gave it a strict inspection, and the draft for the slavish education in the Northeast finally emerged. After the occupation of the Northeast by violent Japan, it tried its best to pick up improper explanations and the fallacy that the Northeast and China were not one. There were even insane traitors who were willing to be used by the enemy, fabricate black and white, and cater to Japan's strange arguments.

Changing the School System

The Puppet State's Ministry of Education has issued a notice to all educational affairs bureaus that, starting this spring, all schools in rural villages, in addition to studying the classics, should pay special attention to studying the Wangdao political and legal system of Japan-Manchuria coexistence and co-prosperity. Furthermore, in the school or spare land, they should cultivate and sow various grains by themselves. As for students who study commerce in cities, they should practice industry outside of class, and their works will be sold by the school or entrusted to merchants. Therefore, rural students pay attention to learning farming, while urban students tend to be industrialized, and they have no time to study knowledge. This is the policy of foolish education implemented by the Japanese.

Japanese and Manchu Languages 173

The purpose of the language training institute for staff established by the Puppet State's Ministry of Education is to teach Japanese and Manchu languages to create loyal and tamed puppet talents. Now, the institute has begun to recruit the fourth batch of students. The Japanese language course is set up in the Changchun Public School, and the Manchu language course is set up in the Machi Elementary School. The two courses are divided into four departments, each of which lasts for six months. The Japanese language course will recruit 480 students, and the Manchu language course will recruit 200 students. School began on March 20.

Raising Tuition Fees 174

Under the instigation of Japan, the Puppet State plans to start raising tuition fees for the next semester of this year. The annual tuition fee for junior high school is 45 yuan (originally 21 yuan), the miscellaneous fee is 12 yuan (originally 3 yuan), and the uniform fee is 20 yuan, which must be paid in full at the time of admission, for a total of 77 yuan. The annual tuition fee for elementary school is 30 yuan, the miscellaneous fee is 7 yuan, and the uniform fee is 20 yuan, which must also be paid in full at one time, for a total of 57 yuan. (Before the incident, the total cost for elementary school per year was no more than 30 yuan.) According to the current price of Northeast soybeans at 1.2 yuan and sorghum at 0.6 yuan, farmers who cultivate 10 mu of land must be in debt of 2-3 yuan. Small farmers are completely bankrupt, middle farmers can still support themselves, and large farmers suffer even greater losses. Based on this situation, violent Japan is raising tuition fees, intending to make those who cannot afford it unable to attend school at all. They will teach those who can afford it with Japanese-made textbooks to enslave them. This year and beyond, children under the age of seven will disappear from the doors of elementary schools.

Setting up a Museum 175

The puppet government has been planning to establish a national museum in Shenyang for a long time, but it has not yet made a concrete decision. With the help of the Puppet State's Ministry of Education, it was decided to use Tang Yulin's former residence on Sanjing Road as the site of the museum. It can be established in April. Yuan Jinkai has been appointed as the curator of the museum and is currently preparing everything.

Number of Students Studying Abroad 176

The puppet state stipulates the system for studying abroad. The students sent abroad are all to cultivate diplomatic traitors. The number of students studying abroad has now been decided: three each for England, France, Germany, and the United States, and 120 for Japan. The reason why the number of students studying in Japan is so much larger than that of other countries is to cultivate more pro-Japanese elements.

France's Boxer Indemnity 179

1. The Motivation for Refund

The movement to refund the French Boxer Indemnity originated around the time of the founding of the Republic of China. At that time, Chinese educators in Europe, including Wang Zhaoming, Cai Yuanpei, Wu Jingheng, Li Yuyi, and Zhang Jingjiang, organized organizations such as the World Society, the China-France Education Association, the Thrift Society, and the Work-Study Society in Paris. Educational undertakings between China and France increased daily, and the public hoped that this would promote goodwill and attention between the two countries, gradually advancing to realize the refund of the indemnity and the undertaking of study.

2. The Mature Period for Refund

In the sixth year of the Republic of China, the European War was in full swing. Because China and France were both allied countries, China was able to defer payment of the indemnity for five years. By the end of November in the tenth year of the Republic of China, the five-year deferral period had expired. Chinese people believed that the time was ripe to initiate a refund movement, and first established the Sino-French University in Lyon with the French side as a preliminary launch. The French government happened to have a plan to decide on the resumption of business of the Sino-French Industrial Bank, intending to refund the entire remaining amount of the Boxer Indemnity, but it was necessary to first use this fund to rescue the resumption of business of the Sino-French Industrial Bank. From then on, the refund measure gradually became concrete.

3. The Sino-French Draft Agreement

On June 24, 11th year of the Republic of China, the French ambassador submitted a note to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs of the former Beijing government. After discussion, both parties agreed to sign an agreement stipulating that the remaining amount of the French Boxer Indemnity would be used to reorganize the Sino-French Industrial Bank and to handle educational undertakings between China and France. Later, the French government again requested that the French Boxer Indemnity be converted into gold yuan (referring to US dollars) for payment. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs rejected this request, but the French side firmly refused to acknowledge this, and the two sides disputed for a long time. By February of the 12th year of the Republic of China, the Beijing government agreed to calculate in gold francs, and public opinion was in an uproar. The National Assembly also opposed it and formally rejected it in a meeting. This matter became a pending case. In the 14th year of the Republic of China, the Beijing government took advantage of the long-term de facto closure of the National Assembly and concluded an agreement with the French ambassador on April 12 of that year, deciding to allocate the French Boxer Indemnity to restore the Sino-French Industrial Bank. Later, the education sector strongly argued, and only then was a small portion obtained to handle education and charitable undertakings between China and France.

4. Total Refund Amount

The total amount of the French Boxer Indemnity refund was 39,158,1529 francs and 05 centimes. Calculated at a legal gold rate of 5.1826 francs per US dollar, the converted amount in US dollars was $75,556,964.457. This total amount was advanced and borrowed annually in accordance with the agreement to the Sino-French Industrial Bank as a fund for the bank to issue 5% US dollar bonds. The Sino-French Industrial Bank then used these US dollar bonds for four purposes: (1) non-interest-bearing securities held by Far Eastern creditors; (2) handling educational and charitable undertakings between China and France; (3) paying the government's unpaid balance of equity capital; and (4) returning various debts owed by the Chinese government to the Sino-French Industrial Bank.

5. Amount Allocated for Educational and Cultural Undertakings

Since the 15th year of the Republic of China, the Sino-French Industrial Bank has allocated US$200,000 annually for handling educational and charitable undertakings between China and France. The handling and distribution methods are negotiated annually by representatives of the French government and representatives of the Chinese Ministry of Education. Therefore, the education sector established the Sino-French Education Fund Committee to manage and distribute this fund, and to complete a kind of permanent fund. It has been heard that many Sino-French educational institutions have been subsidized over the years, such as the Shanghai Sino-French Industrial College, the Lyon Sino-French Institute, the Tianjin Naval Medical School, the Tianjin French Advanced Commercial School, the Paris China College, the Peiping Sino-French University, Shanghai Aurora University, French hospitals in Beihai, Qiongzhou, and Yunnan, the Sino-French Cultural Exchange Publishing Committee, subsidies for scholars to come to China to give lectures, and other Sino-French public welfare undertakings, etc., and the purchase of useful books for public viewing.

6. Committee Organization

The French Boxer Indemnity Committee is named the Sino-French Education Fund Committee. Its organization is composed of representatives from both China and France. The Chinese members are one representative from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, one representative from the Ministry of Finance, one representative from the Ministry of Education, one representative from National Peking University, one representative from National Southeast University, one representative from Guangdong University, and one representative from Sino-French University. The French members are the French ambassador to China or his representative. The above two parties each have one vote during voting. Their functions are based on the Sino-French agreement to manage the Sino-French education undertaking fund and decide its uses.

7. List of Current Committee Members

The Chinese delegation consists of Li Yuyi, Shen Yinmo, Yi Peiji, Liu Xichang (also secretary), Xiao Yu (also resident secretary and staff member of the Chinese delegation), and Xiao Wenxi. The French delegation consists of Wei Dun, Ba Er, and Han Dewei.

Military Training Students from Soviet Central School Conduct Tactical Exercises Yesterday 180

(Zhenjiang, 3rd dispatch) More than 1,300 military training students from secondary schools in Jiangsu Province conducted live tactical exercises at Laoshan outside Zhenbei Gate on the 3rd. They were divided into the North and South armies, departing at 9:00 am. The South army exited the South Gate, and the North army exited the North Gate. Upon arriving at the location, Hu and Gao, the two members of the Military Training Committee, each led their teams to begin combat. Colored flags were used as markers for machine guns and cannons, firecrackers were used to simulate cannons, and firecrackers were used to simulate machine guns. Loud firecrackers simulated rifles. The crackling sounds were as if facing a major enemy. Around 1:00 pm, the two armies met near the small mountain at the southern end of Zhongshan Forest. The commander immediately ordered a gathering for a speech. The team returned to camp at 3:00 pm. Live ammunition shooting will take place on the morning of the 4th, and the awards ceremony will take place in the afternoon.

Ministry of Education Provides Relief to Northeastern Youth Domestically and Abroad 182

The Ministry of Education has established a Northeast Youth Education Relief Office within the Ministry of Education to provide relief to Northeastern youth. The deputy head, Li Xi'en, has been extremely busy in North China preparing for the establishment of Zhongshan Middle School and providing relief to youth who have lost their opportunity to study. It is heard that for the first round of enrollment for Zhongshan Middle School, many people applied for the exam. Several hundred of the applicants were admitted, and the names were announced on March 26. Because the quota is 600 students, more than two hundred students are still needed. It is heard that the second round of examinations is scheduled for April 5. Based on the large number of applicants for the previous exam, the number of examinees for this session should be very enthusiastic. After admission, the students will officially enroll. This is a domestic youth education relief method. It is heard that there are four Northeastern students studying in various countries in Europe and the United States. Recently, they submitted requests stating that due to the fall of the Northeast, their subsidies were unavailable and they requested relief from the Chinese government. The Ministry of Education has ordered the Relief Office to draft relief measures for review and approval. However, the Ministry of Education has already instructed the embassies abroad to investigate the situation of Northeastern youth among the students studying abroad, and after the investigation and reply, to formulate comprehensive relief measures so that the foreign students in general may receive appropriate relief.

Shaanxi Province's Measures for Rectifying Private Schools 183

Shaanxi Province's measures for rectifying private schools have been approved and filed by the Ministry of Education. The original measures consisted of 13 articles. The following is a summary: (1) Anyone planning to establish a private school must fill out a private school establishment application form, along with the qualifications of the teacher, and submit it to the County Education Bureau for approval and issuance of a private school establishment certificate before the school can be established. For private schools established before the promulgation of these measures, an application for approval must be submitted in order to continue to be established. (2) Private schools must meet the following standards: (A) The teacher must have the primary school education qualifications stipulated in the primary school regulations. (B) The curriculum should be based on the primary school curriculum, and at least the subjects of national language, arithmetic (written arithmetic, abacus), common knowledge, and physical education must be offered. Textbooks must be adopted from those edited or approved by the Ministry of Education. (C) The equipment must include at least a lectern, blackboard, and student desks and stools. (3) Each teacher may teach a maximum of 40 children and shall not administer corporal punishment. (4) Private schools that are investigated by the Education Bureau and whose teachers are qualified, whose teaching is legal, and whose equipment is complete may be converted into substitute primary schools or simple primary schools, or short-term primary school classes may be established concurrently, and subsidies may be given as appropriate. (5) The County Education Bureau may establish teacher training institutes as needed to convene teachers who do not meet the qualifications to provide them with strict training. Those who pass the examination after the training period will be issued a teacher certificate and allowed to serve as teachers. (6) Any person who establishes a small private school without approval shall be ordered to close by the Ministry of Education. (7) The County Education Bureau may use winter and summer vacations to organize teacher workshops to convene all teachers in the county for short-term training (the remaining articles are omitted).

Gansu Education Department Director Shui Chuchen Arrives in Shanghai to Discuss the Current Situation of Gansu Education 186

Total accumulated debt reaches 434,824 yuan

Annual deficit of 265,645 yuan

Gansu Province Education Department Director Shui Chuchen recently came south to Nanjing in order to make requests to the Ministry of Education, visited Minister Wang, and presented everything in person. He has already completed his official business and then came to Shanghai for business, staying at the East Asia Hotel. He then went to Hangzhou and returned to Shanghai yesterday. He published a detailed account of the current situation of education in Gansu, which is recorded below:

Number of schools: According to him, there is currently one university (namely Gansu College), fifteen provincial secondary schools, six county-run secondary schools, and one private secondary school. There are eleven provincial higher primary schools, 139 county-run higher primary schools, 64 district-run higher primary schools, and eight private higher primary schools. There are twelve provincial elementary schools, 726 county-run elementary schools, 867 district-run elementary schools, and 79 private elementary schools. There are two provincial kindergartens and one private kindergarten. In total, there is one university, 22 secondary schools, 1,896 elementary schools, and three kindergartens.

Number of students: Currently, the number of students receiving education includes 180 male university students, 1,772 male secondary school students, 128 female secondary school students, 84,571 male elementary school students, 3,716 female elementary school students, and 93 kindergarten students. In total, there are 90,366 male and female students. There are 846,548 children who do not have the opportunity to study.

Sources of funding: Divided into (A) provincial funds, (B) local county funds, and (C) private funds. One university requires an annual expenditure of 96,236 yuan. Twenty-two secondary schools require an annual expenditure of 303,386 yuan. 1,896 elementary schools require an annual expenditure of 324,063 yuan. The total annual expenditure is 723,685 yuan. There are also 287 social public education institutions with an annual expenditure of 3,516 yuan. There are 66 students sent to various universities in the country with an annual expenditure of 11,795 yuan, and one student studying in France with an annual expenditure of 2,880 yuan. In total, the annual expenditure for various educational undertakings in the province should be 849,995 yuan. After deducting the 515,639 yuan from the provincial funds, there is an annual deficit of 265,645 yuan.

Accumulated debt: Gansu is an extremely poor place, and coupled with years of famine, the land is barren for thousands of miles. Often, only 60% of the assessed land taxes and other taxes are actually collected. Taking education alone, the accumulated expenditure debt for the past two years has reached 434,824 yuan. The debt for five middle schools is 147,124 yuan. The debt for four normal schools is 194,835 yuan. The subsidy debt for domestic university students is 18,181 yuan. The overseas student's debt is approximately 30,000 yuan. There are also teachers' monthly salaries, office equipment fees, etc., which have not yet been included.

Remedies: According to him, Gansu is in dire financial straits, and everywhere one turns, the situation is stretched to the limit. The difficulties have reached an extreme. Not only is it impossible to implement plans for improvement, but even consolidating the current situation is hesitant. Due to the lack of funding and the excessive amount of accumulated debt, the equipment in various schools is also becoming increasingly simple and crude. According to Article 20 of the University Professor Qualification Regulations, the attached salary schedule for university professors lists a monthly salary of 400 to 600 yuan for professors, 260 to 400 yuan for associate professors, 160 to 260 yuan for lecturers, and 100 to 160 yuan for teaching assistants. However, the highest salary at Gansu College is 244 yuan per month. Naturally, famous professors cannot be hired. In addition, due to the inconvenient transportation and harsh living conditions, professors who can be hired for 300 yuan per month in the interior will not agree to be hired in Gansu. If the professors are not good, the students' level will also decline. Therefore, in order to seek remedies, the first priority is to improve teachers' salaries in order to hire famous professors. The accumulated debt should be issued in order to add the required equipment.

Returning to Gansu: Shui said that the purpose of his visit to Nanjing was to make requests to the Ministry of Education regarding the above-mentioned issues. He also brought a detailed draft plan for improvement and presented it to the Ministry of Education for review and approval. Gansu College Professor Sun Zhitian, who led Gansu athletes to Nanjing to participate in the National Games, had already returned to Gansu. Sun was ordered to investigate art education in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces and stayed in Shanghai. It is heard that he has completed his task and will return to Gansu with Shui in the coming days.

Schools' Rent Reduction Committee's Letter to Landlords Yesterday 188

Please Voluntarily Reduce Rent

The Municipal Schools' Rent Reduction Campaign Committee sent a letter to landlords of various schools yesterday, stating: "Greetings. Education is a social undertaking. There are thousands of schools in this city, most of which are rented. In recent years, rents have been increasing daily, which has hindered the progress of education. To remedy this, our committee has launched a campaign to reduce rents for schools in the city. This campaign directly aims to alleviate the economic burden on schools, allowing education to gradually develop and improve. This would enable nearby tenants to have opportunities and convenience for their children to attend school, and they would not be willing to move easily. This would also indirectly benefit you, the landlords. Therefore, reducing school rents is in the best interest of you landlords. There are no disadvantages, publicly or privately. It is believed that you will deeply agree. It has been decided by the fourth committee meeting that landlords of various schools in the city should be requested to voluntarily reduce rents, as recorded in the minutes. In addition to requesting the Real Estate Association to provide separate notification, this letter is hereby sent for your attention and compliance. Sincerely, Your Friend."

International Children's Day: Contribution of the World Juvenile Library 191

The World Juvenile Library is a selected translation of popular masterpieces from European and American countries, serving as central materials for children in our country to study literature. The faithfulness of the translation can be said to be almost identical to the original. The freshness and clarity of the writing style is obviously different from traditional storybooks. Illustrations from the original books are included, which can arouse children's interest in reading. According to the editor-in-chief, the entire selection consists of forty-eight types, totaling sixty volumes, published by the World Book Company. The book company is now printing an outline of the World Juvenile Library to be distributed to all sectors. On this International Children's Day, the book company is enthusiastically promoting children's education, changing the original price of thirty yuan and eight jiao for the entire set to a special price of twelve yuan, as a contribution.

Art Magazine Issue 2 Published 192

The ["Art Magazine"] published by Liangyou Book Company, the second issue was published today. The magazine is edited by artists Fang Xuegu and Chen Qiucao, and is the greatest contribution to the art publishing industry in 1934. The format is magnificent and the content is substantial. The entire book uses 120-pound coated paper, with five or six four-color copperplate prints attached. The exquisiteness of the printing is especially rare. This issue includes texts such as Zhu Wenyun's "Random Talks on Chinese Painting," Chuan Lei's "Art Psychology," Lang Lusun's "Overview of Modern French Sculpture," Nietzsche's "Modern Nude Painting," Hua Lin's "Athens of Italy," Sun Zengfan's "Brief History of Western Architecture," and Sun Fuxi's "Salon of the Independents." Literary works include Yuan Mei's "When I Die," Tang Zengbi's "Man and Beast," and Hui Ma's "Poems," among more than ten articles. The pictures include Wang Yachen's color printed Chinese painting "Linhuizao," Zhang Shiguang's "Chrysanthemum Bush and Goose Shadow," Chen Shuren's "Sunset Glow and Qingge," Chen Qiucao's "Secluded Valley and Spring Cold," Chen Baoyi's "Rose and Female Portrait," Bai Ye's "Portrait of a Friend," Lin Zan's "Crab," Fang Xuegu's "Peach-Colored Yearning" and pattern paintings, etc. The cartoons include Jiang Tongliang's "Whipping of Life," Cheng Liusang's "National Law," Guo Jianqi's "Visitors to the Exhibition," Zhang Yingchao's "Gym," and Chen Guangzong's "Artists," among dozens of others. There are also famous photographic works, which are too numerous to mention. It is said that major bookstores in this city and other places are selling it.

Spring and Autumn Children's Weekly Children's Day Special Issue

Children's Day Address 201

— Zhou Shoujuan

Recently, I often have dreams, often dream of my childhood, and I wish I could turn back time and return to my childhood. Why? Because childhood is always happy, and in a heart like a blank sheet of paper, there is never a trace of worry.

But childhood has passed like flowing water, and the flowing water that has passed cannot be recovered, so childhood cannot be recovered either. At present, the only comfort in my soul is to approach children and make friends with innocent children.

I have been editing this Spring and Autumn Children's Weekly for thirteen issues. Every Saturday, when I am selecting manuscripts and arranging them, it is as if I have transformed myself into an innocent child, jumping and running to the children's garden, accompanying the children to swing on the swing, spin the top, tell jokes, and tell stories.

Today, April 4th, is Children's Day, and this year is also our designated Children's Year. How significant is the meaning of Children's Day in this Children's Year! In order to show my respect for Children's Day in the Children's Year, I have specially opened up the entire publication to publish only the works of children, using the spiritual and intelligent articles of the children,

To contribute to the beloved children across the country, I wish everyone will work hard!

Good Spring Scenery 202

— Zhou Ling, Suzhou Jinghai Elementary School

The days are like giant wheels, turning quickly, and the cruel winter is finally overwhelmed by the warm and beautiful spring. Everything also comes out happily to enjoy this mild spring.

The weeping willows by the pond have grown small, tender leaves on their soft branches. From the green water, you can also see the drooping willow branches, which are like a gentle girl, never angry. The withered yellow grass on the ground struggles to produce many fine shoots. When the sun sets, there are always a group of children playing games and telling stories on the grass. The grass seems to be their necessary friend.

Countless swallows, large and small, come in groups, cross the sea, and fly here to make nests on the beams of people's houses. Sometimes they fly out, soaring and carefree in the boundless and pure sky.

When spring arrives, many trees, large and small, are holding flower buds; some have not bloomed, and some have bloomed with lovely flowers for people to admire. The so-called hardworking bee sisters have already been buzzing in the heart of the flowers to collect honey. Fearing that this good opportunity will not return, they are busy collecting countless sweets and taking them home to store. In short, everything that flies and walks on the ground comes to welcome this spring full of joy.

And the spring breeze is so gentle!

Just Don't Forget It 203

— Han Xiaoxia, Shanghai Huanan Elementary School

Mr. Tao, the little joke teller: [Every time I speak to you at the morning meeting, you listen with your east ear and let it out of your west ear, and you never want to remember my words. What is the reason? ··· You have such a lack of memory, I really have no way to help you.]

Student: [Mr. Tao! I have a good idea.]

Mr. Tao: [What idea? Tell me!]

Student: [Just stuff the west ear of everyone with waste paper.]

A gust of wind blows the water, and the water seems to welcome the wind, flowing slightly. It blows the willows, and Mr. Willow sways happily. It blows on people, and people can't help but become gentle. It blows on the flowers, and a burst of fragrance stabs into people's noses. Lovely spring! Don't go back, it is best to stay in the world forever, full of happy air, so that people will not have worries all day and all year round. Spring! Can you do it? Can you do it?

The Warrior's Dream 204

— Tan Xuewen, Attached Elementary School of Shanghai Zhirenyong Women's Middle School

Recently, everyone says that Jie's temperament has changed. That's right! Jie's gentle temperament in the past has disappeared somewhere, and now he is like a wild child running on the street.

Although people say that Jie has turned bad, Jie himself doesn't think so. He only knows that he has started a dream, a dream that is different from the past. What he is doing now is the warrior's dream, and what he did in the past was the good child's dream.

Jie has recently learned to read newspapers. He sees from the newspaper how weak the country he is in is, and this country is not suitable for learning to be a good child. What this country yearns for are strong children who will grow up to fight for the motherland in the future.

Jie believes that every warrior has a violent temperament. Without this violent temperament, this person is not suitable for fighting.

So Jie desperately tries to cultivate a violent temperament, and Jie also believes that every warrior must have a cruel temperament. If warriors are not cruel, how dare they hold the heads of their enemies and laugh! So he first kills some insects, like butterflies, cockroaches, etc., to test his temperament.

The people in the family hate it very much, because they think Jie is too cruel, but Jie himself is very proud.

Although Jie is also a little unhappy, because the people in the family are not as affectionate to him as before. But he comforts himself, he thinks he will always become a warrior in the future, no matter how the people in the family treat him.

So he began to think about learning from Zhao Zilong, the Zhao Zilong who wins every battle, making noise all day long. But this made his family hate him even more, and they said that Jie was getting worse and worse.

But Jie never realized or understood the attitude of his family towards him.

Progress of Human Life 205

— Cui Bin, Anyang Mingxin Elementary School, Henan

The evolution of the species has no end, and the progress of human life has no end: Before the time of Youchao, people ate wild fruits or the meat of birds and animals, drank the blood of birds and animals, lived in caves, and wore animal skins or leaves, but were often harmed by wild animals.

In the time of Youchao, they built nests with wood to avoid harm from wild animals, which was a little more advanced than before.

When Suiren discovered fire, humans knew how to eat cooked food again. Fuxi invented animal husbandry, raising birds and animals to provide food: humans no longer worried about not having food. However, at this time, walking on water and land was still not very convenient.

The Yellow Emperor invented boats and carts, so we humans no longer had to wade through water; we no longer had to walk. Leizu invented sericulture and silk reeling, and human clothing improved a lot!

Now people eat delicacies and delicacies, wear wool and velvet, live in high-rise buildings, and ride flying

The Crows in Xi'an Tell the Time 207

— Ma Zhenhua, Attached Elementary School of Xi'an First Normal School

Since I came to Xi'an for the evening holiday, every day when dusk is approaching, I can always see countless crows flying in the sky, calling and looking for their lodgings. The next morning, they are in formation again, rising up with a loud noise. At that time, I was sleeping soundly, and being awakened by it, I couldn't help but feel a little annoyed, and I always said, where did all these crows come from? At the same time, I didn't pay attention. Who knew it would be useful? It wasn't until I entered school that I realized it could tell the time. In this semester, I relied on it to wake me up on time every day and arrive at school on time. Do the children find this strange? Let me write it out and you will understand.

In Xi'an, there is no standard clock. Although the government strikes a large bronze bell to tell the time every day, it is not necessarily accurate. Therefore, the time of each household is not uniform, and there is a big difference. Naturally, the clocks in schools and homes are also different, and there is no way to make them consistent. It is inevitable that students will be late for school, so my parents deliberately set the clock ahead, but it still cannot be remedied. A few days later, our teacher announced a method, ordering us to pay attention to the crowing of the crows in the morning. When it crows for the first time, we get up, when it crows for the second time, we get up from home, and when it crows for the third time, we arrive at school.

At that time, I didn't believe that crows had the ability to tell the time. Since the teacher said so, I had to obey. Every day I paid attention to the crowing of the crows. The crows in Xi'an do not build nests in trees, but spend the night on the roofs of houses, so every household has them, and when they crow, they can be heard very clearly and can wake people up.

So my mother focused on listening to it for me. When the crow crowed, she woke me up, dressed, got out of bed, washed up hastily, and walked out with my schoolbag. At this time, the crow was indeed crowing for the second time, and I ran to school. It was about to crow for the third time. Continuing like this, it soon became a habit, and I was never late and missed my homework. This proves that it can indeed tell the time.

Poor Old Man 208

— Yu Zhaohua, Shanghai Huanan Elementary School

Once, in the countryside, I saw an old man slowly walking on the road. I asked him: [In this state, where are you going?] The old man sighed and said, I am going to chop firewood. I said, [You are so old, can you still chop firewood?] He said, [I have no way to think. If I don’t chop firewood for a day, I won’t have food to eat for a day.] As he spoke, tears flowed down. ]

I asked him why he didn't ask his son to chop firewood. He said: [My son is very bad. He takes the money I buy every day to drink and gamble. He also has a wife, and I have to support her too! ···]

Alas! The fate of this old man can be regarded as extremely tragic. When I heard this, the water in my eyes couldn't help but burst out. At this time, the old man was also crying and couldn't say anything more. I didn't have the courage to ask him again, and in this moment of sorrow, the old man left without saying goodbye.

The Story of the Sheep and the Wolf 209

— Wang Zechang, Shanghai Minzhi Elementary and Middle School

In the East, there was a fertile field full of tender green grass, where a group of gentle sheep lived, eating grass and living happily every day.

Suddenly, a few brutal wolves came from the East Neighbor, staring fiercely at the sheep, wanting to take them as snacks. The sheep sent representatives to bitterly beg the leader of the wolves: [Mr. Wolf! All things in nature should love each other. We sheep have always advocated peace. Why are you so cruel?] The leader of the wolves sneered: [Hey! Peace! Peace! It is indeed a very pleasant term, but if we take care of your peace, our stomachs will be hungry.] So, in a while, a few wolves tore and devoured a group of peace-loving and non-resistant sheep.

From this story, we can get a lesson and enlightenment: the sheep tried to influence the wolves with peace, but the result was failure. If a group of sheep could seek peace by uniting and resisting, perhaps their fate would not be so cruel! You must know that in the world now, there is no justice, justice is power, and only struggle can lead to final victory!
