Near Vermilion, One Becomes Red 213

— Xu Naiwen, Songjiang Cangqiao Elementary School

When Mu'er was twelve years old, his parents were forced by circumstances and the facts did not allow him to continue his studies. In order to train him to be self-reliant in the future, his parents spent half a year entrusting someone to find a shop in Shanghai and send him to be an apprentice. Mu was a very smart child. In less than a year, he already knew everything about the shop, and his master praised him for his diligence.

Time passed like flowing water, and Mu'er was fifteen years old. He had been promoted from apprentice to partner. But his senior brothers all liked to pass the time by gambling. Over time, Mu'er, who was near vermilion and became red, also became a child who liked to gamble. As a result, he owed a lot of gambling debts.

One morning, Mu'er stole a gold ring from one of his senior brothers. When it was discovered later, he had already changed it into money. After a long period of investigation, he was finally caught by a colleague.

In order to rectify the shop rules, the shopkeeper immediately fired Mu'er for stealing, and his parents compensated for the stolen ring. But his reputation could not be recovered.

Children! Remember that stealing is a shameful thing, reputation is the second life of a person, and also remember the words of the ancients [Near vermilion, one becomes red].

Two Treasures 214

— Zhao Junjun, Shanghai Minsheng Elementary School

What is the most precious thing in the world? I think everyone knows it. That is, the brain and hands that each of us has. Why? Because the brain can think, can invent, and the hands can write and do things. If there is no thought, there will be no invention. Without invention, our society will not progress. If thoughts are not spread through words, and no one does what is invented, our world will not be so brilliant.

Each of us has these two treasures. But although we have these two treasures, we must use them, otherwise it is better not to have them.

The only way for us to use our brains and hands is to read more and learn more, because reading more can make our minds sharp, and learning more can make our hands omnipotent. Therefore, we must read and learn when we are young.

Children get up early every day, go to the yard to practice morning exercises, and after dinner, carry their schoolbags to school. The posture of walking should be as good as in the picture.

A Method for Teaching Young Children to Read 215

— Liu Baozhen, Xinzha Elementary School, Public Works Bureau

My younger brother, Zushun, is five years old this year and naturally intelligent. My father teaches him to read in his spare time, starting from the age of four. By this year, he knows more than a thousand characters, and can explain each one. This is certainly due to his innate intelligence, but also to my father's good teaching methods. I am writing this down now as a reference for home education.

My father teaches my younger brother to read, starting with the names of objects. According to my father, "[Objects are often seen, so they can be easily remembered]." Therefore, before teaching, my father first familiarizes my brother with the object, and then writes the name of the object for my brother to recognize. He only needs to teach it two or three times to be able to recognize it. This method is simple and easy to implement. When teaching descriptive or abstract words, he first teaches him to speak, so that he understands the meaning first, and then writes the word for him to recognize. Therefore, my younger brother can easily recognize any kind of word. I am now writing down this method of teaching young children to read and submitting it to the "Spring and Autumn Children's Weekly" as a contribution to our young friends.

Pattern Painting 216

— Zhou Rong, Jinghai Elementary School, Suzhou

Rocking the Cradle to Awaken the Sleeping Lion 217

— Zhou Shang

It seems that this generation of sleeping lions cannot be awakened, but we should always rock and awaken the little sleeping lions of today. The little sleeping lions of today are the next generation of citizens, the children of today. The revival of our nation depends entirely on the children of today. I hope that the children of today will no longer be like us, so unable to wake up, so inferior to others, so useless. From an early age, we should pay attention to their happiness. The foundation of children's happiness should be built on health. Only healthy children have true happiness, and only happy children can bear the heavy responsibility of saving the country. I believe that the most immediate goal of childhood is to seek the happiness of the children themselves, and the ultimate goal of childhood is to achieve national revival. We should grasp these two points and not let them go easily.

Health is the key to the door of happiness. With this key, any difficulty can be solved. Perhaps from now on, we will not be afraid of foreign devils, and from now on, we will not be afraid of airships and tanks. Originally, "[A nation with third-rate physiques cannot build a first-rate country]," and originally, "[A golden age of culture must be preceded thirty years earlier by a golden age of national health]." The former was said by British Prime Minister George, and the latter was said by American psychologist Hall. These two famous sayings are reflections of reality, and we should think about them deeply. The meaning of health lies in enabling individuals to have a rich life and make the greatest contribution. Children's health must start with three major areas: "[diet]," "[exercise]," and "[rest]." "[The people take food as their heaven]," food is the most important thing, but if food is not obtained in the right way, if one eats too much or too little, if one eats at the wrong time, or if one eats the wrong things, the development of children will inevitably be hindered. Therefore, one must be careful about diet from a young age. Some parents seem to show off and tell everyone, "[Our darling doesn't like to eat green vegetables and tofu]," but in fact, the child actually likes to eat green vegetables and tofu, but as a result of such suggestion, they don't want to eat them anymore. They don't know that vegetables and beans are the treasure of nutrition. Many children fall into the hands of inexplicable things, and don't know how much they are wasting.

To only talk about eating and neglect exercise is called eating for nothing. If you eat but don't get any good out of it, then you have to talk about exercise. Constant muscle activity can enhance the body's developmental power. At the same time, it is also beneficial to posture, digestion, excretion, and mental health. Wise adults should guide them to spend two or three hours every day in fresh air and sunlight, engaging in exercise with enthusiasm. Walking, running, tug-of-war, rope skipping, boxing, mountain climbing, swimming, kicking shuttlecock, and rolling iron hoops are all exercises that don't cost money. Modern parents should understand that children are naturally active, and should let them move. Don't encourage children to wear long gowns and mandarin jackets, and not allow them to move or speak, with a hundred "[no's]," restricting the lively children, making them unable to move, and pretending to have the air of "[old beyond their years]!" Save them! Let them move as they please! Let them retain the spirit of "[hale and hearty in old age]," to struggle for this old nation.

Eating, playing, and working all day long, but not getting enough rest, is still not perfect. Therefore, children should rest when they are tired. Rest is the natural requirement of the body. After doing something for twenty or thirty minutes, one should rest for a while. There is now a proposal that the teaching time in elementary schools should not exceed forty minutes, and each lesson should have a break of more than twenty minutes, which is worth studying. Sleep can also be included under rest. Children are young, so they should sleep more. Ordinary children should sleep with the windows open for thirteen to eleven hours. Sleep helps growth, repairs cells, and restores energy. The more children like to sleep, the healthier they are, and the happier they are. I hope parents will pay attention to this.

Rock the cradle, awaken the sleeping lion, rock it with all your strength, until the lion roars in anger.

Free Talk

Thoughts on Children's Day 218

— Wu Zhiyao

Recently, an author in a famous literary magazine described the scene of his ideal country like this:

"[The city is like a park, with the dense shade of trees protecting the wildflowers. On the clean roads, you can't see a crazy man, a coquettish woman, or a dirty child. Those going to school and those going to work all walk with their chests held high, their faces glowing, greeting each other with an uncontrollable smile, as if everyone knows each other. ]"

"[The blue sky goes away, the starlight gradually appears, and the children are all in warm beds, smiling at the sky in their dreams under the wide-open doors]."

Yes, only in such a peaceful society can there be these happy children.

The mainstay of society is adults, and the lives of adults are bound by countless ingrained habits. For traditional and self-interested reasons, they hate their fellow beings, abuse women, and look down on children. All kinds of mistakes and sins have made people's real lives very painful, and everyone is pursuing a vague future and ideals.

Poor children, some even before they are born, already have sinful elements in their cells. When they come into the world, they are afflicted with incurable diseases for the rest of their lives, or suffer from painful torture, and have to end their lives immediately.

Although most children are called "[innocent]," their "[innocence]" is praised on the one hand, and abused on the other. Suddenly, their black eyes are covered with a layer of dim yellow, and their yelling mouths speak a set of words that they themselves don't understand. Their hands and feet are also locked up. Adults say, "[This child has been educated]."

Now, some people are loudly calling for saving the children, but they seem to have forgotten the society on which the children depend. What kind of society, what kind of children. To save the children, you must first save this society. If we regard protecting children and improving children's lives as the first step in awakening to transforming adult lives, it seems more meaningful to look at Children's Day from this perspective.

Guangzhou Correspondence 219

— Wei Li

XX:

In the past half month, there have been two noteworthy events in Guangzhou: worshipping Confucius and commemorating Guan Yu and Yue Fei. Friend, you are a scholar, so you must be very concerned about worshipping Confucius. Therefore, I will now report this matter to you without fear of being tedious.

Friend, when you hear about worshipping Confucius, you may think that the Confucius here is more prestigious than the Confucius in other places. But in fact, he is just as unlucky. The old man has also been "[not knowing the taste of meat]" for many years. His main hall has long been converted into a military barracks. This time, he suddenly became popular, which was indeed beyond his expectations. Some people say that China is the most mysterious country in the world, and this may be true.

Since the announcement of the Ding Sacrifice on March 17, Confucianists have been overjoyed. They couldn't wait for the day to come so they could pay homage to the Most Sage Teacher. Especially those Cantonese who love to watch the excitement wanted to take this opportunity to visit the Confucius Temple. But in the end, they were very disappointed. On the morning of the Confucius sacrifice, the front gate of the Guangzhou Prefectural School was guarded by soldiers and police step by step. Only officials above the recommended rank or representatives of educational institutions were allowed to enter. I was fortunate to be allowed to enter as a university professor. As soon as I entered the gate, I saw a pair of large lanterns made of yellow paper, with the red characters "[Sacrifice Ceremony]" pasted on them. Entering the second gate, there was another pair of lanterns, with the characters "[Solemn Respect]" written on them. Many seasonal flower potted plants were placed on both sides of the aisle of the Dacheng Hall. A large torch was erected on the left and right sides of the Dacheng Hall. In the center of the hall was the divine seat of the Most Sage Teacher Confucius, with a large horizontal plaque of "[Teacher of All Ages]" as a background. There was a lamp in front of the deity, three large incense sticks, a pair of flower candles, and an incense burner. The sacrificial table was covered with a white cloth, on which were placed tin incense tables, several ancient sacrificial utensils, and a set of three animals [ox, sheep, pig].

At about four o'clock in the morning, the people presiding over the sacrifice were all present. This was the chairman of Guangdong Province, who was the main offering official. This was the director of the Education Department, and this was the director of the Finance Department. They were all secondary offering officials. A little further away, we saw the mayor of Guangzhou and the director of the Guangdong Provincial Public Security Bureau chatting there. They were also secondary offering officials. According to the rules, they were not supposed to participate in the Confucius sacrifice, but as it happened, the director of the Construction Department was concurrently held by the chairman of the province, and the director of the Civil Affairs Department was out on inspection and had not returned. Therefore, the two of them were reassigned to be the secondary offering officials. What an honorable position! Also present were the presiding officials, assistant offering officials, and other accompanying offering officials of the Chong Sheng Temple. They were squeezing around in the crowd.

The ritual of this Confucius sacrifice had already been decided by the Political Affairs Conference. The principle was: "[In terms of spirit, we will restore the sacred canons, while in terms of form, we will not deviate from current etiquette]." Regarding clothing, the main and secondary offering officials all wore formal attire, and the accompanying offering officials wore regular attire. Secondly, during the sacrifice, bowing was performed instead of kneeling, because that was no longer fashionable. But the most difficult problem was music and dance. The ancient tunes seemed to have not been played for a long time, and "[Yi Sheng]" could not be trained in a short period of time. The solution was to invite a local national music research society to play music to add to the atmosphere. As for the rituals such as offering inscribed tablets, offering silk, offering wine, and receiving blessed meat, they were all carried out as before, to show the meaning of restoring the past. At about five o'clock in the morning, the solemn and grand Confucius sacrifice ceremony came to an end.

Regarding the significance of this Confucius sacrifice and its impact, the Guangzhou Minguo Daily editorial on March 17th spoke very thoroughly. I will now excerpt a passage as the end of this correspondence:

"[Since the founding of the Republic of China, there have been frequent upheavals. There has been constant warfare, and there has been no time for civil administration. Moreover, with the rise of heterodox doctrines and the extremism of people's hearts, propriety, righteousness, integrity, and a sense of shame have disappeared. Alas, alas, the solemn and brilliant Confucius Temple, and the solemn and orderly sacrificial rites, have been abandoned for who knows how many years. Commander-in-Chief Chen deeply laments the deepening national crisis and the diminishing of people's hearts. Those evil and lewd things become more and more wanton, and the right path is declining and about to disappear completely. Therefore, he did not avoid criticism and resolutely proposed that all schools should study the classics in the midst of national confusion and fanatical bewilderment. He also reprinted the Classic of Filial Piety and wrote a preface for it himself. Moreover, he carried out the Upper Ding Spring Sacrifice today. How beautiful and glorious! To turn back the tide of the great sea and to purify the eyes and ears of the people. The elders lamented the reappearance of the Han officials, and all the families rejoiced and knew where to return. If it were not for our Commander-in-Chief Chen who aspired to the ancients and had a profound understanding, who could participate in this?]"

Photograph 221

— Bai Yan

While tidying up my bookcase, a photo of Little Lotus from a long time ago fell out of a book. I didn't expect this photo, which had been lost for a long time, to reappear unintentionally. I held it tightly in my hand as if reuniting with an old friend, and carefully examined it: those round eyes, curved eyebrows, small cherry mouth, shallow dimples, and the round face, which was well-proportioned and lovable, all deeply evoked my past memories.

It has been so many years, it seemed like such a spring, when the pear blossoms were in full bloom, the east wind blew the faint fragrance of grass buds, and the initial heat made people feel a little dizzy. At that time, I leaned softly against the fatty bean tree in front of the house, holding a copy of "Dream of the Red Chamber," and reading it with fascination. When I saw:

"[Scattered fallen flowers on the Hundred Flower Isle, fragrant remnants on the Swallow Tower; one after another, forming balls in groups. Drifting and wandering is also like the thin fate of people, empty entanglements, and graceful romance! Even plants and trees know sorrow, and youth turns white. Sighing about this life, who will give and who will take? Married to the east wind, spring does not care, let you go, endure to be left behind. ]"

I couldn't help but silently chant it. I was focusing all my attention on the book, and I didn't know when Little Lotus had also come. It was when I accidentally turned my head that I discovered that she was squatting on the grass not far from me, mechanically stroking the grass with her hands, her head bowed, and immersed in meditation. "[Hey! Little Lotus:]" I called softly.

She didn't answer, just raised her head slightly, and then lowered it again to play with the grass.

So I rolled up the book and walked lightly towards her. I said, "[Little Lotus! Why aren't you paying attention to me!]" and squatted down next to her. But she suddenly turned her head away.

"[Little Lotus! Why aren't you paying attention to me?]" I asked angrily, and rubbed her shoulders with my hands.

"[Paying attention to you!]" She twisted her body and looked at me.

"[Then why didn't you answer when I called you?]"

"[I didn't hear you. ]" She lowered her head and smiled.

"[Okay! You're really good at pretending. I'll call you again now]." I also smiled and deliberately called out loudly:

"[Little Lotus! Little Lotus! ·····]"

Travel Notes of Nankou (Part 1) 222

— He Jie

The motivation for going to Nankou that time was not "[joining the army]," and the result was not bringing back several beautiful poems, embodying courage in gentleness; but because I lived in Beijing, and that place was not far away. It would be a bit unreasonable not to go once. Besides, if I didn't go early, maybe after a year or two, when I wanted to go, I would have to apply for a passport, which would be even more troublesome. So, taking advantage of that good time, I went there once.

Some people say that traveling in China is asking for trouble. In the past, I didn't dare to deny this statement. After going to Nankou once, it further increased my firm belief in my heart.

I got on the train at Xizhimen Station. Fifteen minutes after the scheduled time, the train moved slowly. But before it went out, it suddenly stopped again. I saw railway employees in uniform blowing whistles with their mouths wide open, and armed comrades shouldering guns running back and forth.

It stopped for another ten minutes before it started moving again. Later I learned that the reason was that a regimental commander was ten minutes late, and the train had to wait for him respectfully.

As the train moved, the carriages swayed from side to side, and I felt uneasy in my heart. Seeing the old man sitting on the chair, smoking his pipe and looking relaxed, I realized that my panic was unfounded. They were used to it, and everything was safe once they were used to it, so there was no need to worry. Gradually, I also forgot about the possible dangers, because the fifteen of us, men, women, old and young, were standing there. Although we were surrounded by people, we wouldn't fall down, but standing for a long time made our legs sore, and all our minds were focused on how to get a seat.

I didn't get a seat, so I stood all the way to Changping.

Fortunately, God blessed me. After walking hundreds of miles and seeing the Ming Tombs, I arrived safely at Nankou Station in the evening. The place to stay was the Nankou Hotel. As soon as I approached the door, a rough voice shouted:

"[Stop!]"

I couldn't see anything in the dark, but I saw a flashlight light up, and a dark figure walked towards us. It turned out to be an armed comrade.

One person told him that we were from Beijing and had booked a room at the Nankou Hotel. Only then did he shine the flashlight on everyone's faces and allowed us to enter.

"[Once you go in, you are not allowed to come out. It's a big deal, do you hear?]"

The armed comrade said in a lecturing tone. It was not good to answer, so I could only lower my head and walk inside. When I arrived at the place to stay, there were not enough beds. After negotiation, I learned that many beds were taken away by comrades who were defending the country and protecting the people. We had to share a bed, and each person had to pay one yuan for the room.

I didn't care about those things. The fatigue of the day made me fall asleep as soon as my head hit the pillow. When I opened my eyes, it was already dawn.

"[Oooooh···! Okay! I will answer you now.丨Like calling back a soul. ]" When she said the last sentence, she frowned slightly.

Seeing her like this, I said coldly at the time:

"[You're not happy that I called you, are you?]"

"[Happy!]" She said a little impatiently.

Her strange attitude made me silent. I stared at her without moving, and felt a little unhappy in my heart. After a moment of relative silence for five minutes, she suddenly raised her head and looked at me, hesitatingly saying:

"[I'll tell you!]" But she suddenly stopped again.

Finally, she still lowered her head and said as if to herself; "[No, I'd better not say it. ]"

But her hesitant behavior inevitably aroused my suspicion, and I could no longer bear it, so I shook her body with my hands. As if forcing and begging, I said,

"[No, Little Lotus! You must tell me. ]"

"[I can tell you, but you can't tell anyone else. ]" She said slowly.

I nodded silently. Then she moved her body closer to me. She puckered her mouth shyly and said:

"[Today, Zhang's mother-in-law came to my house to propose marriage for me. ]"

(Her voice was a little vague.)

"[Did your mother agree?]" I asked anxiously.

"[I don't know. ]" She answered vaguely, biting her upper lip. And lowered her head to play with the corner of her clothes.

After hearing this, I was at a loss, and my heart seemed to be suddenly covered with a layer of shadows. With the melancholy eyes of a patient, I stared at the hand playing with the corner of her clothes, motionless.

After a while, I hesitated and said with a slight trembling voice:

"[Didn't my mother tell your mother that she wanted you to be her daughter-in-law?]"

"[That was just a joke. ]" She quickly continued,

"[My mother said, how can people like us be related to your family!···Even if we could, we wouldn't have money to pay for the dowry! ]"

So I became silent again. A stream-like silence occupied our surroundings, and the air seemed to be dead. Before long, she was called away by her mother.

Ah! It has been so many years 丨 Now looking at her beautiful figure, the old tenderness unknowingly returned to my mind again. I slumped in the rattan chair, lowered my eyes and reminisced···

The books were not tidied up in the end, but they aroused a lot of sorrow.

Half a Day's Work (2) 224

— Li Huiying

What does it mean to put these two days together? Is it to thank the friendly nation for its kindness? Otherwise, is it to fawn on the friendly nation in a lowly manner? It has been two years, yes, the second anniversary is unforgettable and cannot be easily buried. For two years, this Guandong Road has fallen into a deeper abyss than before. It seems that the bright days have moved far away. A country that governs with the principle of royal way has been plagued by mutinies and popular grievances in various places it has ruled for a year. Whether in the city or in the countryside, people's livelihoods are hundreds or thousands of times more difficult than before. It is said to thank the friendly nation for its kindness, but that is actually enough. Aren't those people from the friendly nation using the military's force to forcibly occupy other people's land everywhere and oppress good people? They can also do a lot of unspeakable bad things that violate national laws. However, they are, after all, people from a friendly nation, and national laws cannot be applied to them. This gives them a special privilege out of thin air. Enough, I don't want to think about it, I don't want to look at it. The more I think about those things, the angrier I get, and the more I look at the words in front of me, the more anxious I get. 丨丨When will this place be able to regain its freedom?

Continuing to walk, at the entrance of Mongolian Banner Alley, I was blocked by a crowd of people in front.

"[What's going on?]"

While asking myself, I walked to the crowd. The place where people's eyes were focused was a policeman and a bald female madman. After standing for a while, I learned the cause of the incident from people's conversation. It was because the policeman wanted the small shop to hang the national flag. The man in the shop went to the market to buy vegetables, and it happened that this madwoman, the female owner, came to receive the policeman's order. I don't know what happened, but it was nothing more than a disagreement in words, and the two sides clashed. Several streaks of blood flowed from the madwoman's face, naturally from the policeman's ruthless hand. But she was also a true heroine, constantly cursing her opponent:

"[Police dog! You're good! You hit people! I'll settle the score with you! ]"

The policeman stood with his arms crossed, his head tilted, his mouth cracked like a ladle, and occasionally "[hmph]"ed, as if he was showing his noble status to a group of onlookers. It seemed to also contain the spirit of "[you can't do anything to me]".

The police of the new country, since their monthly salary was increased by one national currency note, everyone has been unusually dedicated to their duties and selling their strength, especially to the suffering people. They will show rare majesty. These people seem to have forgotten that they were originally just a subjugated slave and a running dog of imperialism.

I didn't want to waste any more time, so I squeezed through the crowd. However, I can speculate that the result of the incident is that the madwoman will probably still suffer. Of course, it is the madwoman!

I saw the school gate. Two big flags, the Japanese flag and the "[Manchukuo]" flag, were hung crosswise at the entrance. Therefore, the horizontal plaque with "[Jilin Provincial Women's Middle School]" written on it was covered by the flag body, only revealing the three characters in the middle. The preparatory bell rang, urging me to speed up my pace. When I hurriedly walked into the school, the students were all noisily lining up, saying that they were going to the sports field to hold a meeting. I quietly slipped into the crowd. The director of discipline only noticed the chaotic crowd, so he didn't notice my lateness. Looking at the students lining up, few people showed a smiling face. Saying that they were going to attend a celebration meeting, no one really believed it. In their hearts, it seemed that there was a troublesome worry.

The public association's base price for No. 24 coarse granulated white sugar remained at $19.80, and high-grade ordinary Zhuang sugar was at $19.85. No. 8 and 9 Dutch red sugar remained firm. Taikoo Sugar B was at $20.25, with some transactions, an increase of five points from the previous day. Chen Kee's No. 1 fine white sugar was at $18.40, a decrease of five points from the previous day. Numbers 2, 3, and 4 were unchanged. Chaozhou merchants offered a batch of "Jiao Yang" sugar, totaling 200 packages, at $14.85. Previously, the offering price had been above $15.00; it has now fallen by two or three jiao. Yesterday, more Hainan red sugar arrived on Guangdong ships, with high-grade sugar quoted at $13.45, but no transactions occurred. There are currently about 20,000 packages of Chaozhou green sugar in stock, which is not considered a large amount. Because land prices have risen, merchants are unwilling to weaken their position. Therefore, even though sales are slow, asking prices have not been lowered.

Linen and Waterproof Cloth Sell Well 237

Linen and waterproof cloth have been very popular recently, leading to a gradual increase in imports. For summer Western-style clothing, most people are abandoning baratheas and using this material instead. Both local and out-of-town merchants are seeking samples and placing orders, making it more popular than other woolens, linen yarns, and wool textiles. Yesterday, a merchant offered over 400 yards of three-foot linen waterproof cloth at $3.25. Fair Company offered over 500 yards of yellow linen waterproof cloth at $1.05. Tianxiang goods were offered at over 200 yards at $1.125.

Silk and Tea: Shanghai Silk Sales Remain Stagnant 238

(Shanghai Silk Factories to Close) Only a dozen or so silk factories in Shanghai have勉力 reopened after the New Year. Overseas silk prices continue to plummet, and silk is being ignored. The factories that have reopened are likely to close. Currently, only Bao Tai, Yi Er, Yong Heng, Fu Lun, Heng Feng Tai, and a few other factories in the concession and Chinese areas are勉强operating. Most of them are reeling silk抵 for financial institutions. Production will stop as soon as the reeling is finished. The future of silk factories is bleak.

(Factories Have High Costs and Little Profit, Making Sales Difficult) Due to inflation issues in the New York market, raw silk prices have risen, but European and American companies in Shanghai are still trying to suppress prices and purchase cheaply. Chinese silk merchants are suffering significant losses, making negotiations difficult. Domestic silk factories are offering Guangdong silk at around $400, but they have no interest in factory-dried silk. Silk sales activity will take time.

Gongxi Green Tea Sales Slightly Improve 239

The tea market for foreign firms in Shanghai has been depressed for a long time. Electric telegrams were sent out by various foreign firms regarding pearl tea last week, but nothing was learned. However, yesterday, because of demand from Mumbai, Beitou Zhuang, Yulong, and Shengsheng firms slightly improved sales of Gongxi tea. Over 230 chests were traded in the city. The price of goods from new sources was set at $48, while the price of local goods was set at $22, which is an extremely low market. Other goods, such as Xiumei tea, remained unwanted.

Northern Goods and Aged Grain Rice Branches See Prices Decline 240

Due to the poor harvest last year, the glutinous rice branches that arrived were all aged goods. This spring, merchants offering carefully selected high-quality goods once sold them for $130-140. Now, as sales have slowed, the branch prices have eased. It was heard yesterday that a batch was offered for only $82 because it had slight worm damage, a decrease of over $10 from before. Merchants have also lowered prices, and carefully selected good-quality goods were sold yesterday for $100.

Supplement to the Shanghai Local Report

Talk

[Return to Nature] 245

— Qiong Sheng

In this declining society, people's pursuit of pleasure and indulgence seems to have reached its peak. The prevalence of dance halls and amusement parks is a given. But even in cinema, which bears the social responsibility of education, the appeal of alluring sensuality is universally used as a box-office draw. In the past, there was "The Healthy Female," which promoted nudism and reportedly attracted tens of thousands of viewers. Following this trend, two films, "Return to Nature" and "Physical Exercise," have recently been released. The advertisements are full of phrases like "Nude Exercise Photo Special," "Thorough Study of Human Beauty," "A First-Ever Attempt," almost vividly hyping the films. Phrases like "The spring sunshine is bright, don't waste your youth" and "Seize the moment, what could be more enjoyable?" further exert every effort to entice viewers.

Using the promotion of physical exercise or nudism as a shield to satisfy a certain kind of desire in a segment of the population is like adopting the attitude of "I don't care about what happens after I'm gone" from those in a declining social stratum. It's like a person who, nearing the end of their life, gives in to despair before passing away peacefully. Currently, film merchants attracting viewers with scenes of actresses emerging from baths, showing thighs and nipples, is precisely pandering to their tastes and seeking to reflect the prevailing environment. Naturally, this phenomenon causes many moralists to shake their heads and sigh. However, many people flock to it because its emergence and prevalence have deep social and economic roots, and it is not merely due to "the deterioration of social customs and the decline of morality."

Return to nature! Many advocates of physical exercise or nudism are now shouting this slogan, calling for the removal of clothing restraints. We also see many modern women, enamored with nude fitness, echoing this call. Under this bizarre phenomenon of men singing and women harmonizing, is the so-called nude fitness movement the root of all licentious and lascivious events?

If physical exercise does not aim to please men or center on male promotion, it would not be a bad thing to strengthen women's bodies in China, where the aesthetic ideal is the delicate and melancholic Lin Daiyu. This could be the starting point for increasing women's social endeavors. Its content is not limited to the health and beauty of women's bodies, but also includes the nature of women striving for social status and breaking free from family burdens. In breaking down the social system where men control economic power, restoring the gender relations of primitive society can indeed be said to have the meaning of "returning to nature." As for the so-called nude movement, it is by no means the public exhibition of reproductive organs as the promoters and general public in this morbid society imagine. On the one hand, it is to remove the restraints of being adorned with jewels and fettered limbs, and has the purpose of opposing the aesthetic view of women as playthings and the effeminate. On the other hand, it is purely based on physiological hygiene and eugenics to improve women's physical fitness. Exposure to sunlight, sea bathing, and various other indoor and outdoor exercises are of great benefit to removing clothing restraints.

This, of course, is from a scientific point of view. However, in today's society, where women's bodies are commodities on the one hand and "rare commodities" on the other, physical exercise and nude movements have become weapons for some people to "feast on beauty" or achieve certain ambitions. This cannot be explained solely by sexual impulse, but is due to the current environment where "money can make the devil carry a sedan chair," women's economic dependence, and their social subjugation.

This "Return to Nature" movement, it is said, originated in Germany. There are nude beaches in Paris, and it is just beginning to flourish in America. In China, the mere mention of this is as mysterious and rejected as co-education was in the past. Originally, the reproductive organs are not that mysterious. What is mysterious is the ulterior motive of many of those who advocate nudism. It was previously reported that these people had come to Hong Kong and Shanghai to promote it. The torrent of the times is truly topsy-turvy. A few years ago, rumors spread that the Soviet Union was implementing a nude movement and that there was a nude parade in a certain port, which aroused criticism from moralists in various countries, including ours. People suspected ghosts and opposed it as if it were a flood or a beast, but now the movie theaters are heavily promoting it and even imitating it themselves.

But what's so strange about that? There are plenty of people who spout morality and righteousness but secretly act like Ximen Qing from "The Golden Lotus."

Sad Thoughts on Children's Day 246

— Xin

Women and children have always been considered insignificant in China. In the past two years, it seems that there has been a dramatic change. Women have Women's Day, and children have Children's Day. This correction of a mistaken perception is certainly a welcome thing.

This year's Children's Day has arrived again, and social leaders are enthusiastically leading the children in celebrating this joyous occasion. My childhood is already gone. Not only will I not be like today's children, who get a holiday, candy, performances to watch, and a chance to show off their new clothes on this day, but my own era only holds unfortunate and tragic memories. Moreover, even in this era of enthusiastic children's movements, I still harbor unfortunate and tragic shadows for the children of our China! I am not saying this to spoil the fun. It is just that the children in today's society are being taught to be too outrageous. I will first write down some facts to present to our most respected children's movement leaders.

Every day when I return from my office, at the entrance of the alley where I live (in fact, not just the entrance of the alley where I live?), there are always a dozen children, shouting, running, and screaming as they fight. These children are all returning from school after classes. Each of them holds a bamboo sword or a wooden stick in their hand. A more active child holds a metal "sword." Some wear paper crowns and fake beards, and their waists are tightly tied with a belt, just like on the "old opera" stage, except that there are no drums. But while they are pretending to fight, they are making the sounds of drums and gongs in their mouths. It is truly full of murderous intent and very imposing. The child holding the "sword" must be in the upper hand, and the others all pretend to be defeated and kneel on the ground to surrender. Only then does this fierce battle temporarily stop. However, they are reluctant to disperse. They lean against the wall or sit on the cement floor. Some are painting "little five-wheeled vehicles" and "little turtles" on the wall. Some take out square comic books from their pockets to read, "[A flash of white light, and the head disappears!]" "[Riding the clouds and mist, fighting magic weapons in the sky; with a leap, they come and go without a trace]" They are reciting in their little mouths, waving their hands and feet as they jump, as if they are longing to release swords, ride clouds, and fight treasures. The sight of them is so strange that it makes people laugh until they can't straighten their backs.

Every day, I walk a distance to wait for the tram, and there are always several skinny children with sallow faces following behind me, stretching out their little hands and shouting "Get rich, sir!" to passersby, asking for copper coins. When passersby intentionally or unintentionally throw them a coin, they happily pick it up and go to play "hopscotch." Some naughty boys take the coin to the cigarette paper store to buy cigarettes to smoke. Once, I was chatting at the home of a very famous "scholar" in the country. The "scholar's" twelve-year-old eldest son suddenly threw a tantrum and pestered the "scholar's" wife relentlessly, for some reason. The wife indulged her son, calling him her precious darling, and promised to buy him a newly arrived foreign doll with yellow hair and blue eyes to play with. The son still didn't comply and cried, making a fuss, pulling on the "scholar's" wife and hitting her. Later, the "scholar" got annoyed, grabbed the son and slapped his little bottom twice, and shouted loudly at the chauffeur: "A'Er, go call the red-headed A'San and sell him to the foreigners to have his eyes gouged out!" As a result, the son was probably really afraid that the foreigners would gouge out his little eyes, so he was so scared that he held his breath and hid in his mother's arms. The "scholar" then made a silent, ghostly, victorious smile.

These are probably not fabricated jokes, but absolutely true and heartbreaking things! However, there are many more: When watching sensual leg-dancing, they know to sit in the front row; when watching "[Return to Nature]," they will ask, "Why don't they turn around?" They can also help their mothers play mahjong with ten-yuan stakes, buy winning running dog tickets for their mothers, and listen to music and learn social dancing from their fathers. They will also tell their mothers that they want a certain good-looking girl to be their wife... and so on.

These heartbreaking things should harbor great seriousness for the present and future of China! On this Children's Day, when everyone is shouting "Save the children," how should we start to save this large group of young lives? Giving them a day off, holding a meeting, letting them have candy to eat, having performances to watch, and giving them the opportunity to show off their new clothes... surely it won't be that simple to save them, right? If that's the case, isn't that close to a ridiculous deception? It deceives the leaders themselves, deceives the large group of pitiful children, and only leaves them with a deeply ingrained, eternally indelible, unfortunate, and tragic memory when they grow up!

In a film titled "Life Road" that proclaims "Save the children," it also uses ironclad facts to prove that our methods of saving children are terribly wrong!

Postscript to Four Plays Including "Lifebuoy" 247

— Ling He

Spring has arrived, the best season for theater. In the past month, performances have been coming one after another, quite a few indeed. As a theater enthusiast, I can't help but inquire about news related to plays. I heard that the Paradise Theater was staging plays, but I was too busy to go. Of course, I considered this a regret. However, people are like this: having experienced one regret, they must be careful the next time. So, after seeing the advertisement for the "Spring Festival Drama Performance Hosted by the Chinese Women's Cultural Society" on the second morning, I immediately decided that I must go and appreciate it that evening.

If someone asks, "Why are they putting on plays?" then I think it has already been clearly stated in the "Opening Remarks." Moreover, after you have seen the situation at the time, you will naturally understand the respectability of their enthusiasm. If you haven't seen it, then what's the point of saying anything?

I learned from various sources that this was another performance that had not been well prepared. This is the most common shortcoming of the theater movement in China and also the problem that needs to be solved urgently. I have said many times that I have some [blank space] to save it. However, there is no need to discuss it in detail here.

Given the above actual situation, there is no need to be too demanding of everything in this performance. Therefore, I would only like to offer some unimportant opinions below.

There were a total of four one-act plays, including "Lifebuoy," "Wallet," "Father Returns," and "Traitor." Comparatively speaking, "Lifebuoy" should be the best one. In this play, the playwright tells us that at present, the unemployment problem has become the most common and cruel phenomenon. Of course, their best option is to struggle to live on, but there are also a few passive ones who can only end it by jumping into the Huangpu River. However, cruel reality even deprives people of the freedom to die, because this is causing trouble for the police. So, the unemployed worker, who is already mentally disturbed, bravely breaks the glass and takes out the lifebuoy, because he thinks it is enough to save his life. Who knew that this was also causing trouble for the police? Breaking the glass is a violation of the criminal law. Okay, that's how it is. They don't want you to live, but they don't want you to die either; what else is there to say? When the unemployed worker is about to be taken to prison, another group suddenly roars and makes the police feel like they have nowhere to go. This is using comedic techniques to write tragedy, but it is also very easy to become a tragedy and lose the comedic elements. Although the awkwardness of the mentally disturbed unemployed worker is not without its laughable actions. As for the enlightened policeman, he feels unfamiliar, at least there is not enough character depiction.

However, this play is said to have had its script rewritten three minutes before going on stage, so I feel very satisfied. The first attempt is not necessarily a complete success. Several of the main characters, such as the unemployed worker or the enlightened policeman, were played very vividly, especially Wang Yingjun, who had great success in "Rising Moon" and has great performing talent.

Indeed, this play was performed well. In particular, it meets the needs of society; when the enlightened policeman told the unemployed worker to struggle to live on, the audience applauded in unison, showing that it deeply moved the audience. [Blank space].

Page 21

Next, we should mention "Wallet." Regarding this, I have a great feeling: I think this kind of foreign play must be completely adapted. Originally, this is a very rich script, but because the [blank space] and our living habits are not very similar, it is quite difficult to please. No, in a foreign country, in conditions where the audience's standards are very high, it may not be possible to obtain a very great effect, but in China, it is bound to be discounted. The problem lies in the repetitive and verbose dialogue. We must make it clear and understandable. In addition, the performance is not very good, so it is not understood by the audience. Among them, Sha Jun is the best, Vik Jun is the second best, and Hong Dou Jun is the next best. However, if the direction is good, perhaps it can be even better.

"Father Returns" is very familiar to us. Among Kikuchi Kan's plays, this is the only one that can be staged and is full of emotion. It may not be very suitable at present, but based on past experience, it satisfies the tastes of Chinese people. Likewise, this time, although the performance was not very good, several ladies beside me were constantly shedding tears. However, using such an ethical play to trick the audience's tears at present is not really appropriate, is it?

In this play, we do not see a more appropriate direction. In fact, it is said that they only went over the lines once before going on stage. Fortunately, the actors are all experienced, so they can still deal with it.

Finally, regarding "Traitor," I don't want to say anything, because it wasn't finished at all. In short, this performance did not achieve a perfect effect. However, in the absence of good rehearsals, I greatly admire the actors' talents. But, having said that, talent is not the entire property of actors after all. Progressive playwrights should be as careful and faithful to their careers as possible. I wish them hard work!

Masquerade 248

— Jing Jia

I bought a tube of Listerine toothpaste and got a Mickey Mouse mask as a bonus. When I put it on, my six-year-old little sister cried out in fright.

My old aunt, who had just come from the countryside, smiled and scolded, "Why are you wearing a mask? There will be days when you have to wear a mask, won't there?"

This is a common saying in my hometown. It means that those who wear masks are bad people. So, when people see others wearing masks, they will try to stop them.

In the countryside, the characters wearing masks in operas are always the villains. Perhaps this saying comes from that!

However, in this world, who isn't wearing an ugly and terrifying mask? If we just pay a little attention to this society, we can find all kinds of different masks everywhere. Wearing a smiling mask while crying in your heart, wearing a crying mask while laughing in your heart. Strange and bizarre, the entire world is living in masks.

Only when dealing with servants, rickshaw pullers, or beggars do people show their true faces. To gain status, you must wear a mask; to get satisfaction, you must wear a mask. In this world, the usefulness of masks surpasses everything else.

This world is [blank space] with masks! [blank space] one [blank space], some [blank space] I don't [blank space] I aunt [blank space] See [blank space], a fake mask is always [blank space] One [blank space]!

Amateur Mailbox

Starting from Venereal Disease 249

丨Discussion Two

Dear Editor,

Due to the poor social system and the inability of the people to live abundantly, all desires cannot be fulfilled as desired; coupled with the temptations of external material forces, every youth who lacks material things is trapped in a realm of prolonged suffering.

The cause of suffering can prevent you from being self-motivated and lead you down the path of decadence from which you cannot extricate yourself.

In my early years, around the age of twenty, I also committed this problem: smoking opium every day, going to gambling dens, and visiting brothels, not taking it seriously. At that time, my thinking was really strange. Doing this was considered both "dying happily" and "slow suicide." But inside, it was also full of great contradictions. When I lacked financial resources, I still wanted to struggle in order to eke out a living. So, I could only use a small amount of money to try to get a lot of money, so I went to the dice tables and pai gow dens to gamble. If I lost everything, I would go everywhere to find money. Even now, people still say: "You were really outrageous before!"

Now, setting aside other things, the syphilis that worried me day and night did indeed appear one day. My lower body was tingling and very uncomfortable. I knew that this was not syphilis, but a symptom of gonorrhea.

As for the pain during the illness, it was as Zhong Jun Gu Ren said: in addition to the physical pain, I also suffered ridicule from people. At first, I kept it a secret and didn't let anyone know. But how could I hide it when I was walking with difficulty? Finally, my uncle found out, and he said in a warning and sarcastic way:

"Brought back the receipt!"

I could only lower my head, speechless.

I am truly grateful to my uncle, who told me that no matter how bad the environment is, I cannot abandon myself and destroy a strong physique in such a place. Your body is given to you by your parents. Even if you cannot think for the public, you should cherish it for your parents, "[The mother's heart aches during ten months of pregnancy.] Giving birth to you was not easy." Later, he invited a doctor for me and spent half a year to cure the dishonorable gonorrhea. From then on, I focused on doing things and stopped fantasizing. When the lanterns were lit and the red skeletons appeared on the streets, I dared not touch them again.

I have said a lot without mentioning the method of relieving the pain of venereal disease. This is indeed a major social problem. Several years ago, some people advocated banning prostitution. Facts tell me that after banning prostitution without providing work for them, the number of public prostitutes will inevitably decrease while the number of private prostitutes will increase. Now, the only way to address the root cause is to ask the authorities to limit public prostitutes and strictly inspect the prostitutes every week to see if they have any toxic diseases? Otherwise, order them to stop receiving guests.

Aspiring young people, I hope you will still keep yourselves clean. If you have sexual frustration, you may as well exercise and read to relieve it. Whether this is appropriate remains to be taught by experts. I wish you all peace and send my best regards,

Sincerely, Dai Zuichun

Novel

Siamese Ramblings (3) 250

— Yi Min

3. Politics

Siam does not have much culture, and the intelligence of the people is also very low. In addition, the climate is hot, like summer all year round, the land is fertile, and agricultural products are abundant. All the necessities of life, such as clothing, food, and housing, are easily solved. They have no political oppression or economic suffering. Apart from lying in the coconut groves and desperately enjoying themselves, who cares about what kind of world it is now! Therefore, no matter how much the modern ideological tide changes, Siam is still a world of paradise. However, the wheel of history is ultimately moving forward. Since last year, the struggle between civil rights and monarchical power has also begun to become active in Siam.

The first coup was in June of the year before last. The participants were mostly retired soldiers and some incumbent officials. When it was launched, probably because the royal family was unprepared, not a single bullet was fired, and the revolution succeeded within a few hours. After the People's Party seized power, the Siamese king was not removed from his throne, but a parliament was created. At the same time, a constitution was hastily drafted in just a few days. Thus, Siam, which had been an absolute monarchy, was transformed into a constitutional monarchy.

In June of last year, Siam had a second coup. The initiator this time was a group of royalists who had lost power. Their slogan was to overthrow "the current Siamese king, who has no definite purpose, cannot manage political affairs, and allows the people to despise the royal family" (the above is based on the leaflets of the rebels) and to establish "Prince Phra Ong Chao Mom Woranartkul Wimonratana." However, the result was a failure. The political power in Siam is still actually controlled by the moderate People's Party. Recently, I heard that there are new brewing. To what extent the political situation in Siam will change in the future is not something that we outsiders can predict.

Film Special

Prospects for US-Russian Film Cooperation After the US Recognition of Soviet Russia 251

— Cang Sang

Approaching Each Other Is Indeed Possible

Rumor That Von Stroheim Is Going to Russia

Since the United States and Soviet Russia resumed diplomatic relations, Russia's interest in American films and the film market has been renewed. In the Soviet Russian film industry, directors and screenwriters can be heard talking about this everywhere. They believe that scripts based on Soviet Russian subjects will definitely interest Americans, and they often ask some Americans residing in Soviet Russia for their opinions on completed scripts. As for the Russians' excitement, it is due to the sudden activity of American film merchants towards Russia. Since the United States recognized the Soviet Russian government, representatives and telegrams from American film merchants have repeatedly solicited Soviet Russian films. It was not until recently that further expressions of cooperation were made.

However, because both Hollywood and Soviet Russia have had unsatisfactory experiences in previous attempts at cooperation, neither side is currently willing to actively pursue it. Hollywood is well aware that Soviet Russian screenwriters are unwilling to erase the communist life within Soviet Russia and create something else. Therefore, if American film merchants are eager to change tastes but unwilling to promote Soviet ideology, then Soviet Russian film figures on the private side can only suspend activities and wait for the opportunity. If American film merchants cooperate with the Soviet Russian government on films in Russia, they will also encounter the same difficulties. However, despite this, many figures inside and outside the film industry believe that although Russians have had various failures in the past when they brought Soviet Russian ideology to Hollywood to make films, it is now very likely that Hollywood and Moscow will reach a compromise.

According to the Russians, American film merchants are well aware that there are many novel film subjects in Russia. Using American film techniques and Russian artistic theories to develop Russian materials will definitely yield excellent results.

The Moscow film industry was very excited to hear the news that Erich von Stroheim had petitioned the Soviet Russian government to allow him to work for a Soviet Russian film company. The Russians greatly admired von Stroheim's art and unanimously felt that if he could come to Russia, then with his genius and his experience in the United States, there would definitely be good results.

Film Review 252

Review of [All of Me] 253

— Ling He

ALL of Me 丨 Grand Light

First of all, I believe that the most commendable aspect of this film is the director's extremely serious attitude and the highly cinematic artistic expression. Perhaps the name James Hood is still unfamiliar to us, but his directing technique is truly astonishing.

I believe this film should be used as a blueprint for our reference. The entire film is so clear and understandable. It extracts such rich drama from an extremely simple story. Without being verbose or piling up details, it concisely and clearly presents everything that should or must be expressed. In particular, there are three very brilliant scenes that we may as well study in detail.

When the film begins, the director sets up an extremely tranquil scene in order to depict the sweet love between the male and female protagonists. (1) Night, a beautiful garden. A high-angle shot captures the man and woman lying on the ground. (2) A medium shot of the man and woman lying on the ground. (3) The sound of a bell, the camera moves out, a flower dissolves. (4) The bright moon. (5) Then, returning to the male and female protagonists. | This depicts the time from dusk to moonrise. And the sweet words between the lovers are vividly displayed on the screen, inspiring endless envy.

After the male protagonist angrily leaves the female protagonist's home, she sits in place drinking coffee. Her mother enters and asks, "Forgotten him? Is he gone?" "I don't know," the daughter replies with a melancholy tone. Then, the mother asks, "So what do you plan to do?" She replies, "Me? ...I'll drink my coffee." This is the beginning of the unfolding of a new plot, and in these cold few words, the female protagonist's abnormality after losing her lover is fully expressed. But this is not enough; in the immediately following scene, the director depicts her inner feelings as follows: (1) The female protagonist sits alone in contemplation. (2) The maid brings in breakfast, the woman eats a little, then tells the maid to take it away. (3) The woman is melancholic, restless, and goes to the window. (4) She retreats from the window and sits down in her original place. (5) Her mother enters and comforts her daughter. (6) The mother leaves, and the daughter remains silently and restlessly. (7) The maid hands the woman a letter, and the woman tells her to make a phone call. (8) The woman makes a phone call, holding an unopened letter in her hand. (9) A close-up of the front of the envelope. (10) A close-up of the letter. The following dissolves to a sanatorium. | This scene handles the female protagonist's inner changes extremely well. Simple and clear in a static atmosphere.

Next to mention is the climax of the drama. (1) Fast-paced shots of the exterior of a tall building. (2) The fugitive Ani and his lover Eva are in a room, talking anxiously and urgently. (3) Someone is knocking on the door; Ani and Eva are suspicious and dare not open it. Then they hear the name of Sister Li, and they open the door to let her in. (4) Sister Li gives Eva a bag, telling them to escape quickly. (5) Suddenly, they hear urgent knocking on the door; the three are at a loss. Ani and Sister Li go to the door. Eva asks who is outside the door and learns that it is the police who are capturing Ani. (6) Ani goes to the window, preparing to jump, and hears the noise on the street outside the window. His lover urgently embraces him. (7) The knocking becomes more urgent. Noise. Ani explains to his lover. (8) Eva is noncommittal and gradually loses consciousness. (9) Ani puts one foot on the window sill. Sister Li is by the door, watching, and then shouts loudly. (Ani has jumped) The noisy voices of people on the street. (10) The sound of police whistles and ambulances on the street. Sister Li covers her face with her hands. (11) Eva has a dazed, painful expression and decides to jump out of the window to commit suicide. (12) Sister Li leans against the door, watching the window, then stands blankly facing the wall. Noisy shouts on the street. (13) The police break down the door and arrest Sister Li. | | It can be said that this scene fully demonstrates the author's cleverness. What is most noteworthy is that when the first person jumps down to commit suicide, it is shouted out by the female protagonist, but when the second person jumps, it is explained by the voices of people on the street. Neither time do they directly show their posture of jumping out of the window. As for the latter, it is even better to first show Sister Li's unwillingness to watch. What is even more worth learning is the atmosphere created at the time: tense, dense, beyond compare. For example, first depicting the height of the building is actually telling you in advance that those who jump out of the window to commit suicide will surely die.

Well, as mentioned above, the director's technique is truly amazing. In addition, the actors all perform extremely well, so formally speaking, it is truly an excellent film. And the crisp recording and the beautiful photography are just extra details.

Now what I want to talk about is the content of the film.

Here, the playwright raises the question of whether passionate love and marriage are consistent. Originally, this is almost beyond doubt and is not worth specifically raising. However, the playwright first emphasizes that passionate love does not necessarily lead to marriage. That is to say, passionate love is one thing, and marriage is another. When Professor Tang is moving due to work and asks his lover to go with him and get married, she says: "What I want is not to marry you, what I want is to love you, to love you forever... That's so different!... (Passionate love and marriage) I think our love will die from marriage..." This fully depicts the female protagonist as an idealist who believes in the supremacy of passionate love. Later, the playwright uses another poor couple to illustrate that before marriage, there needs to be true love and, even more so, a full understanding of each other. Finally, he tells us through the mouths of the male and female protagonists: "Let's go to Paris for a while." The female protagonist, Sister Li, replies: "Let's go, let's go to the West. At this time, I have completely changed my mind." That is to say, passionate love should have its responsibilities, and marriage, bearing and raising children, is the final stage of passionate love, without a doubt. Furthermore, before marriage, there must be a full mutual understanding and true love, and even if it means sacrificing oneself for passionate love, it is worth it.

Naturally, this is very much to the taste of the petty bourgeoisie. What exactly is true passionate love and marriage built on? We think of the poor couple in this way: they understand each other, they truly love each other, but society does not allow them to live. Although they still struggle for their future children, the harshness of the law, under the so-called name of thief, they commit suicide one after another. So, good results can only be enjoyed between university professors and young ladies. Perhaps this is the playwright's subconscious expression, but we cannot help but have the above feeling.

Random Talk About Wireless Radio Movies 254

— Ji Yang

Home radio receivers can now be seen in major cities in China. In the near future, wireless movie projectors can also be installed in our homes. We only need to turn on the switch, and we can comfortably watch a favorite sound movie in the living room. This has already started in New York, USA. It is said that the installation fee is about 125 US dollars. If the silver price rises now, we will only need to pay the price of a five-tube radio to install a small home sound theater. Isn't this both novel and cheap?

However, because of this change, I am afraid that the film industry will undergo drastic changes as a result. First, on the part of filmmakers, in addition to continuing to produce films, they will also have to add [sound] and [broadcasting] theaters, and of course their business will also increase. Second, movie theaters will be the first to suffer, because many people can watch movies freely at home, in trains, steamers, hotels, etc., without taking a step out of the room, and the business of movie theaters will of course suffer a major blow. Third, on the part of the audience, they don't have to wait [with bated breath] for new movies, but there is also a drawback, that is, the movie (being broadcast) cannot use outdoor scenes. This is very regrettable. I wonder if it can be improved in the future? Fourth, actors will also be affected in three ways: (1) Blondes - their color is not clear when printed on the screen. (2) Redheads - red hair has no color when printed on the screen. (3) Those with rough voices will be eliminated. According to the test results, black and pale complexions look best when filmed. In this way, black-haired girls such as Dolores del Río, Norma Shearer, Swanson, and Joan Crawford will be blessed with luck. Red-haired girls, such as Howard Keel, Jenny Gaynor, and Nancy Carroll, may be abandoned.

Makeup will also be affected: lipstick will have to be changed to blue, and powder will have to be changed to white. The beards worn by male characters will have to be changed to green glue or green powder. So every event has its advantages and disadvantages, isn't that just wireless movies?

Film Novel

Carolina (12) 255

— Wen Yin

After a while, Joanna said: "Oh, so this is what's done in the great and solemn Connelley Mansion... All good, all honorable... So vicious... Specially ruining people's lives. Well, I don't want your land. If so, I still have to run away quickly. I don't want to see such a person again in my life." Will stood at the door, blocking the way and not letting her leave. He said, "Joanna, you don't have to have that kind of thought... That's the past, it's already dead... We have our future!" Joanna said sadly, "You and I have no future." Will said, "We have a glorious future. I have prepared everything." Joanna said, "I don't believe it. You used to tell me you loved me... I don't believe it anymore. You should go back to Charleston and get married..." Will glanced fiercely at his mother, then said to Joanna, "Joanna, there is only one person in the world I want to marry! That's you!" But Joanna shook her head sadly and said, "I don't believe it, let me go. Your mother is right - she is always right. It was right for her to ruin my grandmother's life, too. It is also right for her to prevent you and me from being together. It is especially right for her to drive me away from this terrible place. She told lies - said your uncle died - of course, that was also right..." Before she could finish her words, a terrible sound suddenly came from outside, interrupting her words. Giraldine shouted, "What's wrong?" Shouts of alarm arose outside, and only Scipio's voice was heard, saying: "Oh, God save me! Poor Mr. Robert has committed suicide!" Will and Giraldine ran out in terror. Mrs. Connelley collapsed into a chair, holding her head in her hands. Joanna looked at her once, then slowly walked away.

Everything was packed and loaded into a box. Joanna stood in the stripped-down room, looking around. She could not help but feel sad, and tears streamed down her face. After a while, she urged her younger brother, "Jack, hurry up, the car will be here in a while." As Jack closed the lid of the box, she saw the printed cloth dress she wore when the Connelley family had a dance last time... It was only a short while ago! Will... It was so easy to meet, and so quick to lose him! So she bit her lip tightly, not letting it tremble. After a while, her older brother Harley asked again: "Sister, where are we moving to?" Joanna said almost tearfully: "Far away..." A broken carriage had already arrived at the door. The black driver helped Joanna, Harley, and Jack carry everything to the carriage. Joanna's hands were groping blindly, and her eyes were blurred with tears. Suddenly, someone shouted at her beside her, startling her. It was Li, the owner of the grocery store. Li looked at Joanna's sad face from above his glasses and said, "What does this mean? Mrs. Connelley can't do anything to you. I have checked the law. According to the law, you can live here until the next planting season. By that time, who knows how the world will have changed." Joanna did not answer him. She silently walked back into the house and looked around to see if there was anything left behind. (To be continued)

Home
